Hebei Jingxing Mine Investigation Record (2) 82

The entire mine has three coal shafts, so-called, which are the paths for extracting coal and the routes for coal miners to enter and exit. No. 1 shaft is located in the southern part of the mining area, excavated in the 28th year of the Guangxu reign, and converted from a rectangular shape to a circular shape in the 3rd year of the Republic of China. It was renovated once in the 7th year of the Republic of China, with a depth of 184 meters. Each time, it hoists 1.3 tons of coal, and 600 tons every eight hours. The coal from the first layer underground is transported out from this shaft, but the coal mining area of the first layer is gradually shrinking, and the transportation route for coal from other layers is too far. Based on the current situation, its coal transportation lifespan is no more than five or six years. No. 2 shaft was excavated in the 30th year of the Guangxu reign, in the northern part of the mining area, 400 meters from No. 1 shaft. Initially, it was used to extract the coal from the first and second layers, and later, for ventilation, it was excavated to a depth of 184 meters. The shaft opening is circular, and each time it hoists 1.3 tons of coal, and 800 tons every eight hours. Currently, the coal from the second and third layers underground is extracted from this shaft. The entire mine's drainage and air outlet also utilize this shaft, but the shaft is not straight, which not only wastes materials but also often causes danger. It is now planned to stop coal extraction from this shaft and use it exclusively for workers to go up and down, as well as for drainage and air outlet. No. 3 shaft is located in the northwestern part of the mining area, 1,740 meters from No. 1 shaft and 1,520 meters from No. 2 shaft. It was excavated in the 13th year of the Republic of China and completed in the 18th year of the Republic of China. This shaft has the best construction, with a depth of 250 meters. A 1,000 cubic meter long reservoir was excavated underground, and a new 1,600 meter long reservoir was excavated in the fifth layer of the tunnel. This shaft is equipped with a large water pump (pronounced as 'pound', i.e., a water pump), which can pump 3,000 liters of water per minute. The coal extracted from the fourth layer, which used to be transported by No. 2 shaft, has now been changed to be transported by the North Shaft, which can hoist 1,300 tons of coal every eight hours. The coal transportation railways all lead directly to the shaft openings. The underground coal mining methods are roughly divided into three types: one is the room and pillar method, the second is the natural caving method, and the third is the backfilling method. The room and pillar method is the most common method for coal mining. Although the natural caving method saves labor and is efficient, it often causes injuries due to caving, and a lot of coal is discarded as it falls with stones. The backfilling method is now being used.

The entire mine's machine motive power is divided into three locations. The hourly steam production of the boilers is 17,000 kilos. There are four generators with a capacity of 394 K·V·A. The important machine parts are as follows: (A) Seven winches, located in various places underground and on the ground, with three types: steam-powered, electric-powered, and compressed air-powered, depending on the location where they are installed. No. 1, 2, and 3 shafts and the winch rooms each have a steam-powered winch, specifically for hoisting coal, lowering materials, and for workers to go up and down. The first layer material road, the third layer dark shaft, and the fourth layer dark shaft underground each have a compressed air-powered winch, used to transport coal to the 184-meter-deep level tunnel, and then transported out of the shaft opening by the ground winch. (B) Water pumps. Two horizontal water pumps are installed in the tunnel 184 meters from the ground to discharge water directly to the ground. Each pump operates for 22 hours per day. One vertical water pump discharges the water from the bottom of the well to the tunnel 132 meters from the ground, and then a horizontal water pump continues to discharge it to the ground, operating for five hours per day every day. Last year, a double steam-powered horizontal pump was added at the lowest point of 254 meters underground. This machine pumps 3,000 liters of water per minute. (C) Ventilation equipment. There are two old exhaust fans, one with an exhaust capacity of two cubic meters per minute, and another with 800 cubic meters per minute. A new 180,000 cubic foot fan and a 450-horsepower steam engine have also been installed. No. 1 shaft has nine boilers, No. 2 shaft has eleven boilers, and No. 3 shaft has four boilers. More than 300 electric lights are installed underground, and more than 1,700 are installed on the ground. Three telephones are installed underground, and 32 are installed on the ground.

The entire factory is divided into two main sections. One section specializes in repairs, and simple manufacturing is also done occasionally. The other section manages the use and maintenance of various machines, such as coal extraction and transportation. The existing machine tools include only seven lathes, two planers, two drilling machines, one iron sawing machine, two wood sawing machines, one wood lathe, one mechanical forging hammer, one wood planing machine, and one iron rolling machine. The work in the factory is roughly divided into four categories: 1. Smelting and casting (mold making, sand casting, etc.); 2. Cold metalworking (filing, lathing, planing, riveting, cutting, piercing, drilling, flattening, rolling, etc.); 3. Hot metalworking (forging, casting, etc.); 4. Woodworking (all kinds of wood materials, tools, etc.). According to Secretary Su Changgeng, who visited the mining area, the various equipment in the wood mine is relatively complete, but the lack of drinking water facilities underground is a shortcoming. The summer season is approaching, and the workers are sweating profusely. The daily demand for drinking water has increased sharply compared to the winter. If water cans are transported by manpower, it is difficult to supply them adequately. Director Fu pays close attention to this and has decided to install drinking water pipes underground to provide workers with sufficient drinking water. (To be continued)

Wuhu Express News 84

Before the issuance of the Anhui Province Rice and Grain Public Bonds, a rice and grain export inspection office was established. Now that the one-million-dollar rice and grain public bonds have been implemented, the inspection office has been abolished.

The Fifth Rear Hospital of the Army, located in the old town government office in Wuhu, has been in operation for a year. Recently, it received orders to move to Hankou. All wounded soldiers will be transported to the Beijing-Hankou sanatorium or returned to their units. Director Wu Linsheng, upon receiving the order, is actively winding down operations and is scheduled to begin transportation tomorrow.

Bandits were discovered in Dangtu. The 57th Division dispatched a team to surround and disperse the bandits. Several people were killed on the spot, and bandits Yu Changyue, Lu Dezheng, and others, seven in total, were captured. They were escorted to Wuhu today for interrogation. (11th)

All sectors are preparing to build Sun Yat-sen Park. A preparatory meeting was held at the county magistrate's office at 2:00 PM today. Dozens of people attended, including the county government's public security bureau, construction commissioner, and engineering commissioner. It was decided that Li Boxing's Great Road and Great Garden would be used as the park site, and engineering commissioners Zhang Zhongfu, Duan Tianzhen, and others, five in total, were appointed to be responsible for the preparation.

Businesses have repeatedly objected to the issue of affixing stamps to the bills for the three festivals. Recently, the Stamp Tax Bureau still strictly ordered stamps to be affixed to the bills, otherwise, penalties would be imposed. The County Chamber of Commerce believes that the bills are of a notification nature, and very few payments are received immediately after a bill is issued. If stamps are affixed every time, it would be a double tax, which is contrary to the constitution. Therefore, it has sent a circular to all guilds to unanimously oppose it. (12th)

Local Communications

Nanhui 85

Bandit Shen Xingmin Executed by Firing Squad Bandit Shen Xingmin, on the night of the 16th of March in the 18th year of the Republic, colluded with Zhou Heqing, Wang Wenqi (who have already been executed), and Yang Zanchu (who has repeatedly evaded capture), to kidnap Dong Wencai, the son of Dong Yuanzhang, a farmer in the Xi Sanjia area of Yituan. On the night of the 20th of March in the 19th year of the Republic, he colluded with Wang Jinsheng, Yang Zanchu, Chen Liangchu, Shen Lanyi, etc. (who are on the run), to kidnap Wu Guangxing, a farmer in Zhunan Township. On the night of the 13th of November of the same year, he colluded with Pan Xiangyun, Ding Gehua, Ding Afu, Shen Aqing, Gu Heyun, etc. (who are on the run), to kidnap Shen Guanjin, a merchant in Erzaohong Town, and killed Shen. The county government interrogated him, and the confessions were confirmed. He was sentenced to death and reported to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for approval by telegram. Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, the prisoner was brought out of prison, his identity was verified, and he was escorted to the execution ground outside the South Gate and executed by firing squad.

Songjiang 86

Jinshan's wanted bandit brought to justice. County Magistrate Jin recently received a confidential report stating that a bandit named Ni A'gen had committed numerous crimes and was hiding in the Nanma Peng area of Datinlin due to strict arrest warrants. The police captain Chen Rongchu was ordered to lead a team to arrest the bandit at the address and bring him to the county government. After investigation, it was learned that he was a wanted bandit from Jinshan County and should be brought to justice. A formal document was prepared, and a political police officer was dispatched today to escort the bandit to Jinshan County for investigation.

Citizens petition for drinking water. Recently, County Magistrate Song Wei has been constructing cement and steel bridges at Zhugan Huidongwai and other places. Zhu Bingji contracted the project from the Construction Bureau through bidding. However, to seek convenience for his own work, he cut off the river channels at the bridge construction sites. People objected at the time, but he ignored them. In recent days, the water flow has been blocked, and the river water smells foul. Citizens believe that the bridge construction will take time, and if the dams are not removed and the flow allowed, epidemics are feared. On the morning of the 13th, dozens of citizens went to the county government with banners to petition. County Magistrate Jin summoned the heads of the Construction and Public Security Bureaus and ordered the contractor to quickly remove one-third of the dam. The contractor agreed to do so, and the citizens were satisfied and left.

Chuansha 87

Sea bandits kidnap and murder. Xujialu Town in the northern part of the county borders the sea to the east and Baoshan County to the west. At about 9:00 PM on the 10th, more than a dozen sea bandits suddenly arrived, each armed with pistols and Mauser pistols. They first robbed Huang Tongchang's general merchandise store of more than 400 yuan. Then, they went to Xia Changshun's fish store and kidnapped the owner Xia Hanglin and the shop assistant Cai Genbao. At the same time, they fired shots to show their power, intending to loot the store. At that time, the Public Security First Branch stationed in Gu Town (about four li from Xu Town) happened to dispatch two patrol officers to patrol near the town. They suddenly heard gunshots and stopped and fired into the air. The bandits heard the sound and fled in all directions. However, Zhou Tulin, the owner of the Zhou Xiesheng butcher shop in the town, had a five-shot pistol at home. Hearing that the bandits were fleeing, he chased after them with the gun and fired at the bandits. The bandits turned around and returned fire. He was shot in the left leg and fell to the ground. The bandits jumped forward, snatched the gun, and beat him severely with the gun butt, then threw it into the river. He died instantly. The bandits then went into the butcher shop and kidnapped the clerk Chen A'mao and fled with shouts. By the time the detectives arrived, the bandits were far away. The body of Zhou Tulin, who was shot and killed by the bandits, was fished out of the river. His body was covered with scars, a truly tragic sight. On the 12th, County Magistrate Tu, along with Examining Officer Huang, went to the countryside to examine the scene. As for the fish shop owner Xia Hanglin and the other three kidnapped, there has been no news to this day.

Suzhou 88

County clerk commits adultery with a maid. Peng Gengzi, a clerk at the County Middle School, had a love affair with a maid named Wu Erbao and lived together. In June of last year, she gave birth to a boy. On December 15th, Wu Erbao's uncle, Chen Bingchu, because Erbao's original spouse was surnamed Bian, planned to hold a wedding. So, Chen's wife, along with Erbao's mother, Wu Xue, went to Peng's house and dragged Erbao away. Peng Gengzi then filed a lawsuit with the local court, accusing Chen Bingchu and others of obstructing freedom. The criminal court judge Wang Dawei presided over the trial and ruled that Chen Bingchu and others were not guilty. However, the prosecutor disagreed with the ruling and appealed to the High Court. Yesterday (13th), Judge Zhao of the Second Criminal Court held a hearing. The plaintiff, Peng Gengzi, was ill and did not attend. Only Wu Erbao testified in court, stating that her mother and uncle did indeed obstruct her freedom. Subsequently, Prosecutor Sun Xiheng made his arguments. The trial concluded, and the verdict is scheduled to be announced on the 18th of this month.

Detective team captures abductor. Shen Mingbao, the seven-year-old daughter of Shen Xiao'si, a tea boy at the Suzhou Orphanage, was abducted by abductors Yin A'san, Qian Yin, etc. in February of this year and sold to the Zhu family in Runyu Lane, Lao Laji Bridge, Shanghai, for thirty yuan. Later, Shen Xiao'si received a letter and reported it to the detective team for investigation. A relative of Shen Xiao'si named Qian A'wu was captured and sentenced by the local court to one year and two months in prison. Yesterday, detectives captured Qian Yin on Hulong Street at lawyer Lu Xiangru's house and Yin A'san outside Xumen. They were immediately taken to the bureau and transferred to the local court for investigation.

Measures to eliminate lake bandits. The Wu County government previously planned to work with the water and land police to first eliminate the bandit lairs in Tian Da Tan, Da Fu Dun, Xin Kai Lu, Shen Jia Lu, and other places in Taihu Lake, and then thoroughly investigate the straw shed tenants along the lake, and formulate strict measures to eliminate banditry. After reporting this to the Civil Affairs Department for approval, an instruction was received yesterday stating that the plan was essential and should be discussed and implemented conscientiously, and detailed rules for cracking down on the lakeside tenants should be drafted and submitted for review.

Five Jing Bang bandits rob and injure people. On the night of the 11th, at 2:00 AM, Zhou Shengqing's house in Wu Jing Bang, Guangfu City, was robbed by lake bandits, and Zhou and his son A'rong, as well as villager Cao A'shui, were shot and injured. They carried the stolen goods towards Taihu Lake. The injured Zhou Shengqing and others came to the city yesterday (13th) for treatment.

Wuxi 89

Jiangsu Provincial Water Police to be reorganized. The news of the reorganization of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Public Security has been circulating for a long time. Now, we have received confirmation that the Civil Affairs Department has decided to reorganize the six water police districts in the province into three branch bureaus, with a general bureau to oversee everything. The plan is as follows: 1. The original first and fourth districts will be merged into the first branch bureau, with the bureau headquarters located in Wusong. The current chief of the first district, Xu Pu Cheng, will be appointed as the branch bureau chief. 2. Wuxi's second district and Suzhou's third district will be merged and reorganized into the second branch bureau, with the bureau headquarters located in Suzhou. The current chiefs of the second and third districts, Shen Gao Chen, will be appointed as the branch bureau chief. 3. The fifth and sixth districts will be merged and reorganized into the third branch bureau. The current chief of the sixth district, Cheng Zhuang, will be appointed as the branch bureau chief. The general bureau will be located in Minhang, Shanghai, and Jiang Chao Xiong has been appointed as the bureau chief. This plan has been decided to be implemented on July 1st. After the reorganization, it will be divided into inland river and offshore departments. The inland river department will be responsible for suppressing the Taihu Lake bandits, and the offshore department will be responsible for suppressing the Yangtze River pirates. Measures have also been formulated.

Silk factories oppose tax on cocoon traders. The issue of collecting business tax from the cocoon trade was previously discussed by Director Yang of the Business Tax Bureau, along with Qian Sunqing, chairman of the County Chamber of Commerce, and Hua Shaochun, chairman of the Cocoon Trade Association. The cocoon trade argued that they were requesting the ministry and province to exempt them from the tax, but had not yet received a response. Moreover, the silkworm season was terrible this year, with only one or two percent of the usual harvest. In fact, it was impossible to add this burden. The director of the Business Tax Bureau, however, stated that the department's orders were strict and could not be delayed any longer. He demanded that the recognized amount be determined first and then start collecting the tax. After repeated discussions, it was decided to recognize an amount of 3,500 yuan. However, yesterday, Yongtai, Qian Sheng, Zhen Yi Cheng, Zhen Yi Xie, Ding Chang, De Feng, Tai Fu, Zhen Feng, Yi Feng, San Tai, Yu Feng, Cheng Feng, Qian Feng, Rui Chang, Yuan Kang, and 15 other silk factories, argued that fresh cocoons purchased in Jiaxing, Zhejiang, and Wu County, Suzhou, were not subject to business tax. Why should Wuxi be the first to collect it? The trade association should seek benefits for the industry. How could it comply with the Business Tax Bureau's intentions and hastily recognize the amount? They immediately sent a letter to the Cocoon Trade Association, stating their opposition and refusing to recognize the recognized tax amount.

Gu Wangyi of Bancun Township kidnapped. Gu Geng Shang, a small village in Bancun Township, tenth district of this county, has a resident named Gu Wangyi, who is over fifty years old and has a small amount of land, barely enough to make a living. However, he was coveted by bandits. At about 3:00 AM the day before yesterday (12th), five or six bandits suddenly arrived, carrying guns and flashlights, broke open the gate of Gu's house, and went straight into the inner room. They did not rob anything but dragged out Gu Wangyi, who was already asleep. Without even putting on his clothes, he was surrounded by the bandits and taken away. Afterwards, his family reported the incident to the district office, which in turn reported it to the police team stationed in the township, requesting a rescue.

Large number of refugees cause trouble in the countryside. Yesterday (13th), more than a hundred refugees, men and women, suddenly arrived at the Da Ci An near Yangjian Town in the eighth district. Most of their clothes were gorgeous. Several leaders of the refugees claimed to the people in the temple, "We want to borrow some travel expenses from you." The temple holder replied that they had no money. The refugees were furious and rushed in, looting extensively. After an hour, they looted more than 200 yuan in cash and two dan of white rice and carried them out. The next morning, the refugees pawned six fur robes at the Kangji Pawnshop in the town for more than 100 yuan. They were spotted by the members of the 28th detachment of the business corps, who saw that they looked flustered and interrogated them. The refugees hesitated and stammered, and a pawn ticket was found in their bags. They were immediately detained and reported to the detachment leader, who immediately sent more than a dozen corps members, armed with guns, to escort the refugees towards Yanqiao. In Dongqiao Town in the ninth district (Beishang Township), fifty or sixty refugees also arrived. The township chief issued them food rations. However, the refugees went to the Xinbaoji Deyin nunnery and robbed it of dozens of silver dollars. Then, they went to the home of a farmer named Ji Huzi in Liubanqiao Township, claiming to be thirsty and asking for tea. Ji believed them and gave them a cup of hot tea to quench their thirst. After the refugees left, his neighbor said that the refugees had an abacus. Ji heard this and immediately went into the room to check the box. Sure enough, 80 silver dollars were missing. He immediately went outside to look for them, but the refugees had long disappeared and could not be found.

Party department investigates private settlement of opium case. Xue Chunxian, a resident of Li She Town (Qingcheng City) in the fifteenth district, smoked opium, defying the current ban. Local people reported this to the 15th Public Security Branch for investigation. However, the branch chief not only did not send police to arrest him but instead sent Shen Jinfu, an outsider, to collude with local ruffian Xue Chaojing to bribe and settle the case privately. The fifth district's third sub-department learned of this and considered that the branch chief dared to accept bribes and settle the case privately, which was corrupt and derelict of duty. The truth should be investigated. Therefore, yesterday, they submitted a request to the higher-level party department to investigate the matter. At the same time, Public Security Director Xu also detected the news and planned to send someone to the countryside to investigate.

Changzhou 90

Robbery and injury near Hutangqiao. At about 11:00 PM on the 11th, more than 20 bandits suddenly arrived at the home of Zhang Chunshun in Tiandafang Village, Xiaoliu Township, near Hutang Township, Wu County. They surrounded the house and fired shots to show their power, then broke into the house and looted. Zhang's wife, Ji, was tied up and burned with a straw raincoat all over her body, suffering serious injuries. Her seventeen-year-old daughter was also beaten and injured. After an hour, the bandits shouted and left to the north. After checking the losses, it was estimated that more than 300 silver dollars and about 500 yuan worth of clothing and jewelry, as well as more than a dozen land contracts, were stolen. The next day (12th), Zhang Shunshan sent his wife to the city for treatment at the Wujin Hospital. According to the doctor, she was not yet out of danger.

Bandit Wang Zhengshu captured in Suzhou. Tang Renjie, chief of the ninth public security branch in Butou, Wu County, previously worked with the business corps branch to uncover a robbery plot by Li Si and other bandits and seized three stolen ships, four pistols, bullets, silver ornaments, and other items. However, Wang Zhengshu and Wang Zhengfu were still at large. It was reported that they had fled to Suzhou. Xu Shaoyun, the deputy captain of the Qingxiang Bureau's detective team, was secretly dispatched to Suzhou and captured Wang Zhengshu at the Fu'an Teahouse. He was escorted to Changzhou on the 12th. Wang Zhengfu escaped without a trace.

County court executes bandit by firing squad. The Wu County Court previously received a bandit named Zhu Jinsheng, who confessed to kidnapping Wang Jusheng and Wang Jinzhao and extorting ransom. He was sentenced to death and reported to the High Court for transfer to the provincial government for approval and execution. Upon receiving the order, the court brought the bandit Zhu Jinsheng to court at noon on the 13th, verified his identity, and escorted him to the Fenghou mound execution ground for execution by firing squad.

Jiangyin 91

Heavy soil case criminals escorted to Suzhou. The Wu County Local Court will hold a hearing on the opium bribery case of former County Magistrate Li Leng and former Examining Officer Yang Ying tomorrow (15th) at 1:00 PM, and has issued summons to Huang Bingying and others to appear for questioning, as well as a supplementary summons to Xi Yinzhen and his son, important figures in the case. On the 12th, the county government ordered bailiff Wu Bowen to escort the three prisoners Wu Shanbao, Qian Abao, and Lu Longbao to Suzhou to await interrogation.

A murder case takes a turn. Wu Rukang of Tangjiaqiao, Qiaoqi, was murdered by Wu Axi's son last year, suffering thirteen knife wounds. The county government arrested Wu Axi and has been detaining him for seven or eight months. He was sentenced to one year and six months a few days ago. However, Axi's wife and daughter-in-law all went to Rukang's house the day before yesterday and beat the widow Wu Feng almost to death. Yesterday afternoon, they went to the county government to report the incident for investigation.

Yangzhou 92

De Kang Bank robbed. De Kang Bank, located on the middle street of Gaojiaqiao, in the northern part of the town of Fairy, under the jurisdiction of this county, was broken into by more than a dozen bandits who held guns and robbed the place. All the valuables were looted, and they fired their guns on the way out before calmly scattering. The bank owner, Ding Yao, has reported the incident to the Fourth Public Security Bureau for investigation, and the branch has turned over information to the county government who will instruct the police to track down the thieves.

Gaoyou 93

The bandit leader Tao Wenfu was escorted to Gaoyou: Xu Bin, the Chief Detective of the 6th District of the Public Security Team stationed on the waterways of Gaoyou, previously captured the bandit leader Tao Wenfu in Zhenjiang. He was sent to the Provincial Public Security Bureau under custody. After Director Cheng prepared a document ordering Inspector Wang Baoqing to escort him, he was escorted to Gaoyou last night and sent to the district headquarters for interrogation.

A rural woman's urination leads to a snake entering her abdomen: Zhang, the wife of Hu Wenxiang, a villager of San'e Town in the county, was urinating in the field the night before last when unexpectedly a snake of about two feet long entered her abdomen through her vulva. Zhang was in great pain. She immediately returned home and sought medical treatment, but the doctor could not save her. It is reported that her life is in great danger.

A hurricane sweeps away two people: Gao Deshun and Hu Zhicheng, two farmers in the southern countryside of Baoying County, were transplanting rice seedlings in the field at about 3 pm the day before yesterday when suddenly a strong wind arose, sweeping them both into the air, and their whereabouts are unknown. They have not yet been found.

Nantong 94

Deep-water port villagers resist arrest and cause a disturbance: The Construction Bureau is requisitioning labor to expand the Jiangbian revetment of the Deep-water Port. The villagers strongly oppose it. At 5 pm on the 11th, Director Feng Mufu invited County Police Captain Jin Juechen and others to the county government for secret discussions on arresting the ringleaders. At 8 pm, two large vehicles carrying more than 40 armed police officers drove to search and arrest them. They arrested 15 people including Ni Pangzi and Wang Lin in Ni Jiayuan and Wang Jiayuan. Just as they were being escorted onto the vehicles, the villagers rang gongs, and in an instant, six or seven hundred people gathered, each holding farm tools to resist arrest, hoping to rob the arrested people. They smashed the vehicles. The police opened fire as a warning, wounding four people including Zhou Jishi, Chen Pan, Qian Lin, and Shi Pan. The crowd then dispersed. The 15 people including Ni Pangzi were escorted to the county government. On the morning of the 12th, the villagers carried the wounded men and women to the court to request an autopsy and to the county government to request the release of the 15 people in custody. Because County Magistrate Zhang had gone to Jinsha to inspect district affairs and had not returned, there was no result, and they dispersed.

Qingjiang 95

A rural farmer loses his life due to a misunderstanding: Zhang Shaomei, a farmer from Shuangjin Gate in Huaiyin, 29 years old, was harvesting wheat in the field on the 7th when he saw troops passing by. Zhang mistakenly thought the troops were conscripting laborers, so he put down his farm tools and ran away in a hurry. The soldiers saw Zhang's panicked appearance and suspected that he was a bandit, so they opened fire. The shot hit Zhang in the waist, and he fell to the ground immediately. Zhang's family heard the news and rushed over, hurriedly carrying him to the Benevolence Hospital in the port for treatment, but due to the severity of the injury, he could not be saved, and he died on the morning of the 9th.

Continued report on the tragic murder case outside the city: Regarding the case of Wu Shi, a tenant of Lu Kairong's family in Taipinggang Alley outside Huaiyin City, Hebei, who was assassinated on the night of the 7th, it has been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that the Huaiyin County Government dispatched Shen Cheng, the judge, and Shouling, the judicial secretary, and others to the scene of the incident for investigation and examination on the afternoon of the 9th. It was determined that Shi had three gunshot wounds on the left temple and around the ears of her face and was killed. Because no family members of the deceased were present, Jiang Lianke, who rented the house, was ordered to hand over Shi's husband, Wu Yinhou, to the authorities for investigation.

Jiaxing 96

A police team's gambling arrest leads to a fatal case: In Tangjiagang, near Liubaimu Dang on the border of Jiaxing and Jiashan, various gangs of gamblers opened a large gambling den there. The Jiashan County Government, considering that the area belonged to Shan territory, ordered You Sixian, the captain of the patrol team, to lead the police to arrest them. Captain Xu believed that the area was only separated from Jiaxing territory by a river and feared that the gamblers would flee into Jiaxing territory when arrested. Therefore, on the afternoon of the 12th, he personally went to the Jiaxing County Public Security Bureau to report the reason and asked Director Gao to send police to assist. Captain Luo led four patrol officers and accompanied Captain Xu on the No. 1 patrol boat to arrest them. The gamblers fled one after another. At that time, Hu Xueyin was running from Tangjiagang to Hudiegang, already half a mile away. The police officers chased him hard and shot him with a wooden-shell gun, causing Hu to be shot three times and killed on the spot. The other police officers arrested Shen Lianshou, Cai Xiong, Li Deyi, and three others. Captain Xu handed them over to the Jiaxing police team to be escorted to the Jiaxing County Public Security Bureau for temporary detention. Hu's body was carried back to Qianjiaqiao in Tanghui by his family. On the 13th, they reported the case to the Jiaxing and Jiashan County Courts for an autopsy and filed a complaint requesting compensation.

The Wangjiangjing water police rescue a hostage: Meng Yiliang's family, who ran a clothing business in Dongshoubang, Tianningzhuang District, on the border of Jiaxing and Jiashan, was robbed by bandits on June 5th. Before leaving, they kidnapped Meng's wife, Fei, who has been missing ever since. Until yesterday, the Wangjiangjing water police learned that the hostage was hidden in Shenjiadou, Wangjiangjing District. The squad leader immediately led the police to search Wu's mansion in the area and found the female hostage. The bandits had already fled upon hearing the news. The female hostage is now being escorted to the Xitang team headquarters for investigation.

Hangzhou 97

A major fire in Taipingju Alley: Taipingju Alley in the Houshi Street of Hangzhou is a small alley inhabited by ordinary poor families. There are six buildings at No. 17, occupied by eight families including Jiang Binghong, Guan Peiran, Li Hongsheng, Zeng Xinglin, Chen Jifu, Jiang Baoting, Jin Dingjun, and Wang Jinshui. Around 9 pm the night before last, Jiang Pan, the mother of the Jiang family, accidentally set fire to the mosquito net while using a lamp to catch bedbugs, and the fire blazed fiercely, making it inaccessible. Fire trucks from various fire brigades and various Jiyi dragons rushed to the scene to put out the fire, which was extinguished at about 11 pm. After investigation, a total of 24 houses in the alley were burned down, affecting 31 households, with a total loss of more than 14,000 yuan. Jiang Pan, who is old, suffered burns on her hands and feet, but fortunately, no one else was injured. The police from the First District have detained Jiang Pan's son, Binghong, for temporary custody, and he will be transferred to the Public Security Bureau for investigation after interrogation.

A bandit executed by firing squad in Hangzhou: Shen Zengfu, a bandit from Deqing, previously robbed and kidnapped people for ransom in the county. He was captured by the water police and sent to the province, where the High Court found him guilty and sentenced him to death. This morning at 8 am, he was escorted to the Qingbo Gate execution ground and executed by firing squad.

Anqing 98

Foreign sheds of foreign steamships in Xiangkou are ordered to relocate: Xiangkou Town, located 120 miles upstream of Anqing in Dongliu County, has foreign sheds set up by the Nichi-Qing and Jardine Matheson companies for steamships to stop, load, and unload passengers. Recently, the provincial government, based on the report from Yang Ying, the magistrate of Dongliu County, claimed that the foreign sheds forcibly occupied civilian property. Additionally, based on the report from Zhou Shantong, the director of the Provincial Ship Management Office, the steamships of the two companies often privately transported military supplies and red pills, unloading them in the town. It was requested that this be banned. Therefore, the county magistrate and the Xiangkou Public Security Bureau were instructed to order the Nichi-Qing and Jardine Matheson companies to relocate the foreign sheds within a limited time and to prepare a plan for alternative transportation, requesting the Ministry of Communications to review and approve. Yesterday, instruction No. 2720 from the Ministry of Communications was received, stating that since the foreign sheds set up by the Nichi-Qing and Jardine Matheson companies have now been ordered to relocate within a limited time, efforts should be made to supplement them to facilitate transportation. In addition to ordering the China Merchants and Sanbei companies to handle this matter as soon as possible, they should be informed.

Wuyuan 99

Box tea is changed to business tax collection: Box tea exported from the county to foreign firms was previously subject to special collection by officials sent by the Finance Department. Since the implementation of tax reduction, the tea tax bureaus in various counties have also been abolished. All box tea is now subject to business tax. The Qimen and Shanghai Tea Industry Associations have successively sent telegrams to the Ministry of Finance requesting exemption, which has been approved for reduction. Now, the County Tea Industry Association has received an order from the province, forwarded from the Ministry of Finance, to collect 5/1000 of the capital amount. After receiving the order, the association convened a meeting of all tea merchants to discuss the matter. They all stated that collecting based on the capital amount was inaccurate and proposed collecting 1.4 jiao per box to avoid disputes arising from disagreements over the amount. Li Kangmin, the commissioner of the business tax district stationed in Qimen, Yixian and Wuyuan, recently sent a Mr. Hu to Wuyuan to start the investigation and asked all tea merchants to stamp and register in advance. Once the investigation is completed, the collection will begin.

Education News

Important news

Procedures for Establishing Secondary Schools in Various Counties and Cities 104

The Ministry of Education has formulated procedures for establishing secondary schools in various counties and cities, and issued a circular to the education departments of various provinces, which states:

It has been found that the number of graduates from higher primary schools in various counties and cities is gradually increasing, and the governments of various counties and cities have successively opened secondary schools to meet the needs. However, there are no clear regulations on the establishment procedures, which has led to inconsistencies in handling. The procedures for establishing secondary schools in various counties and cities are hereby formulated. In addition to distributing them separately, this order is hereby issued to the department, and you are hereby instructed to forward it to the counties and cities under your jurisdiction for compliance. This order includes a copy of the procedures for establishing secondary schools in various counties and cities.

Procedures for Establishing Secondary Schools in Various Counties and Cities 105

Article 1: When counties and cities (cities under the jurisdiction of the provincial government) open secondary schools, the competent educational administrative organ shall first prepare an explanation and methods based on the following points and submit them to the provincial education department for review and approval. (1) A list of the number of graduates from higher primary schools in the entire county or city in recent years, a survey of the total number of students entering higher education, and the number of students entering secondary schools and various vocational schools. (2) If there are public or private secondary schools in the county or city, the operation of each school and the enrollment situation should be reported. (3) If there are public or private secondary schools in neighboring counties, the operation of each school and the distance between it and the proposed secondary school should be reported. (4) A list of the number of schools, the number of students, and the amount of funding for primary schools and mass schools in the county or city, and the number of out-of-school children. (5) What kind of secondary school is proposed to be opened. (6) The local need for the proposed secondary school to be opened. (7) Source of funding and a budget of recurring expenses for regular operation. (8) A plan for school buildings and various equipment and practical work sites. (9) Expansion plan after opening. (10) Career plan for students after graduation.

Article 2: The provincial education department shall review the reports submitted by the counties and cities, and may send personnel to investigate if necessary. If the review results meet the following points, the counties and cities shall be allowed to prepare for establishment. (1) The enrollment situation of graduates from higher primary schools in the county or city makes it necessary to establish the secondary school. (2) The source of funding is stable and the amount is sufficient for use and does not encroach on the local inherent education funding. (3) The school buildings and various equipment and practical work sites are sufficient for application.

Article 3: When establishing secondary schools in various counties and cities, priority should be given to opening vocational schools such as agriculture or industry.

Article 4: Within six months after the establishment of secondary schools in various counties and cities is approved by the provincial education department, the following items should be prepared and submitted by the county and city governments for record. (1) School organization, staffing, and various articles of association and rules. (2) School building floor plan. (3) Statement of income and expenditure of opening expenses. (4) Curriculum. (5) Catalog of textbooks and reference books. (6) Catalog of books, instruments, and specimens (if there is an affiliated factory, a catalog of machinery should be provided). (7) Sports and hygiene equipment. (8) Resumes of the principal and faculty.

Article 5: The provincial education department shall report the approved secondary schools established in the counties and cities to the Ministry of Education for record.

Article 6: The provincial education department shall assign inspectors to inspect and guide the secondary schools established in the counties and cities at any time.

Article 7: The secondary schools established in the counties and cities shall be under the direct supervision of the county and city education bureaus or education sections.

Article 8: The establishment procedures for district-level secondary schools in districts below the county and city shall be regarded as the same as those for county and city-level secondary schools and shall comply with these procedures.

Zhejiang's New Budget for the 20th Year 106

Income: 21,178,957 yuan Expenditure: 27,246,301 yuan

Deficit: 6,067,344 yuan, which will be offset by a discretionary allocation from old debts and public bonds.

The Zhejiang Provincial Government, in view of the fact that the reliable income of the province in the 19th year was only more than 15 million yuan, while the expenditures listed required more than 38 million yuan, and the arrears were accumulating, since the reorganization of the provincial government last December, after Chairman Zhang Nanxian took office, similar duplicate organs were separately merged, various expenses were repeatedly reduced, and various organs were ordered to prepare and submit the income and expenditure budget for the 20th year in accordance with the provincial government's austerity policy, so as to match income and expenditure. Therefore, after the budget meeting of the provincial government committee decided to reduce the budget, the relevant competent organs first prepared and sent detailed budgets to the finance department, which then carefully reviewed them. Then, the finance department invited the accounting personnel of the competent organs to attend a meeting to discuss and re-reduce the budget. However, the relevant educational organs did not submit detailed figures for the reduction, and although the original budgets submitted were slightly changed, the total amount was generally the same, so they were still included in accordance with the original budgets submitted. The new budget for the 20th year, which has been compiled by the finance department overnight, is estimated to have an income of 21,178,957 yuan and an expenditure of 27,246,301 yuan. The difference between income and expenditure is a deficit of 6,067,344 yuan. All the insufficient funds will be offset by a discretionary allocation from the 8 million yuan of public bonds issued to clear old debts. Yesterday, the finance department had submitted the above budget to the Zhejiang Provincial Government Committee for discussion.

Zhejiang Finance Department Plans to Issue Arrears of Education Fees 107

Education fees for March, April, and May will be paid in one lump sum.

The Zhejiang Finance Department received an order from the province to raise and issue the second half of the February education fees, which was previously reported in this newspaper. It is now known that the Finance Department, considering the difficult lives of educators and the end of the semester, has decided to take advantage of the start of tax collection in various counties and the relatively strong income from land taxes to issue education fee notices for March, April, and May in one lump sum, so that all new and old debts of education fees can be completely cleared. It is also heard that it has been decided to send the aforementioned notices to the education department tomorrow (the 15th) so that they can be transferred to the relevant educational organs for application.

Central University Establishes Department of Health Education 108

Nanjing, 13th Telegraph. The Department of Health Education jointly established by the Ministry of Health and the School of Education of Central University will begin enrolling students in the fall of this year. The examination subjects for July 13th and 14th are Party Principles, Chinese, English, Physics, Chemistry, Biology, and a special physical examination. Students with a high school diploma or above are eligible to apply. The admission qualifications for overseas Chinese and Mongolian-Tibetan students can be handled flexibly. There are also three scholarship amounts, each with a scholarship of 50 yuan per semester, which is qualified for those with the best academic performance and recommended by the professors' meeting.

Local news

Municipal Education Bureau Prepares for Summer School 109

The preparatory committee for the second session of the summer school of the Municipal Education Bureau has been appointed to five people, including Jiang Hongqi, Zheng Tan, Ma Chonggan, Li Heshu, and Chen Yiqing. They are now actively preparing. After the bureau affairs meeting decided, according to the regulations for in-service training of primary school teachers, the qualifications for this year's summer school entrants are: (1) Graduates of the Department of Education, School of Education, or Normal University; (2) University undergraduates (excluding the Department of Education), graduates of advanced normal schools, senior normal schools, or normal specialty schools; (3) Graduates of vocational schools (excluding advanced normal schools); (4) Graduates of senior high school normal departments or normal undergraduates; (5) Graduates of rural normal schools with a study period of more than four years. The courses offered are (A) Required courses: (1) Primary school administration and moral education issues; (2) Provisional standard test experiment research on primary school problems; (3) Child psychology; (4) Attention symbols; (5) School health; (B) Elective courses: (1) Outline of primary school Party Principles teaching materials; (2) New plan for primary school work courses; (3) Guidance methods for primary school extracurricular activities; (4) Teaching experiment methods; (5) Testing and statistics. In addition, there will be three lectures every week, starting from July 13th to August 2nd, for a total of three weeks. It is also heard that those who serve as teachers in Shanghai municipal primary schools and meet the above qualifications will be given corresponding punishment according to the in-service training regulations if they do not attend summer school without reason.

Da Xia's 7th Anniversary and Graduation Ceremony 112

Da Xia University held its 7th anniversary and graduation ceremony yesterday (the 13th). More than 2,000 guests including Xu Peihuang, Zhu Jingnong, Zhu Yingpeng, Hu Shuhua, Li Zhaohuan, Chu Fucheng, Xu Peikun, Zhao Yunwen, faculty, and Da Xia graduates attended the ceremony. Parade (Qichang photo)

The meeting started at 9 am, and the ceremony was held as usual. President Wang Boqun was unable to attend due to attending the Fifth Plenary Session of the Central Committee. Vice President Ou Yuanhuai represented the chairman and delivered the opening speech, stating that the school was established only seven weeks ago, and the scale is still rough. Judging from the meaning of the school's name Da Xia University (that is, the university of Greater China), it is still far away. I hope that all teachers and students of the school will remember the name and strive together with the spirit of cooperation and struggle to achieve our goals. As for the responsibilities of the graduating students, they are very important. According to recent statistics, there are only more than 17,000 students in national and registered universities in the country, that is, only one person in 20,000 people in our country enters university. Compared with European and American universities, where one school has as many as 10,000 to 20,000 students, there is a vast difference. However, university students are criticized, saying that one more graduate means that the family has one less useful son, and society has one more unemployed person. In all fairness, our country's politics is not on track, and society is in chaos, making it impossible for university students to have a proper way out. This is really not the fault of the university students themselves. How should you overcome this harsh environment to seek a path to self-reliance in the future? Only your own efforts are considered. Next, Wang Yuxiang reported on the progress of the school in the past seven years. Zhu Jingnong then spoke, stating that students graduating is like a ship launching into the water. From now on, the sea is vast, and the future is full of dangerous waves. One must have a fearless spirit. Chinese university students often suffer from having nothing to do after graduation. In fact, there are many things that can be done, only if you can find your own way. I hope that you will work hard in all aspects of society in the future and not only tend to politics. Next, degrees were awarded, songs were sung, and music was played, and the ceremony ended. In the afternoon at 3 pm, various ball games were held, and at 7 pm, there was a grand variety show. It is estimated that there are 7 graduates from the School of Liberal Arts, 2 from the School of Science, 58 from the School of Education, 5 from the School of Business, 21 from the School of Law, 53 from the Advanced Normal Department, and 88 from the Preparatory Department.

Daxia Almost Sweeps China-Japan Track and Field Competition 115

Best Performance in 100m Hurdles

School Record in 1500m

|Japanese Residents Excelled in High Jump and Hurdles|

|Daxia Volleyball Defeats Jinan Three Sets to Two|

Yesterday, Daxia University held a China-Japan track and field competition to celebrate its 7th anniversary. Simultaneously, there was a volleyball match between the university and Jinan University. The Patriotic Girls' School volleyball team also came to participate and cheer. Due to the late hour, it was difficult to gather the Daxia women's volleyball team, so it was cancelled. In the China-Japan competition, Daxia scored 79 points, and the Japanese residents scored 47 points, resulting in a Daxia victory. In the volleyball match, Daxia also defeated Jinan three sets to two. People are in high spirits during joyous occasions. It is fitting for everyone at Daxia to be motivated and accomplished during this anniversary.

Six Heroes Shine for a Time 116

Yesterday, the China-Japan meeting at the Lida River attracted the attention of the general public. In the twelve events, Daxia dominated with nine first places, while the Japanese residents only had one first place and two shared first places (because the Japanese residents requested it, the order was not determined according to the usual rules). Daxia's excellent performance was truly astonishing. When discussing merit and rewards, the six heroes should be commended first. The six heroes are He Debao, Li Shaoshang, Long Zexian, Chen Baoqiu, Luo Chuanxian, and Wu Jinqi. He Debao's 11.52 seconds in the 100 meters and Luo Chuanxian's 17.51 seconds in the high hurdles were the best performances in each event. Long Zexian's 4 minutes and 56 seconds in the 1500 meters was a new school record. The Japanese residents were almost defeated everywhere. Fortunately, Furukawa single-handedly supported Daxia, excelling in both the high hurdles and high jump.

Comparison of Competition Scores 117

Daxia Track Events: 35 points; Field Events: 44 points

Japanese Residents Track Events: 26 points; Field Events: 21 points

Total: Daxia 79 points; Japanese Residents 47 points

Daxia Volleyball Wins 118

Defeats Jinan Three Sets to Two

The Daxia volleyball team competed against the Jinan volleyball team at 4:00 PM. At the beginning of the match, Daxia's captain, Chen Baoqiu, was absent due to participating in the China-Japan competition. During the intense battle, Jinan showed great momentum, winning two consecutive sets with scores of 21-12 and 21-10. Daxia was in a critical situation. Captain Chen personally joined the ranks, and the entire team rallied. The situation changed. In the subsequent three sets, Daxia won consecutively with scores of 21-14, 21-17, and 21-17, resulting in a victory of three sets to two. The referee was Lu Xiangqian.

Amateur Basketball Tournament in City No. 1 Venue

"Bomber" Team Wins God Group Championship 128

The amateur basketball competition at the City No. 1 Public Sports Venue saw the two powerhouses of the God Group, the "Bomber" team and the "Nanguang" team, compete for the championship yesterday afternoon at 4:30 PM. The "Nanguang" team had good coordination, while the "Bomber" team displayed exquisite skills. Each team showed their strengths in stealing the ball and shooting baskets. However, basketball is a team sport, not an individual one. Despite the "Bomber" team's strength, they initially fell behind in the first half with a score of 8-11. In the second half, the "Nanguang" team, filled with pride and impatience, directly attacked with the ball, each player wanting to score points, resulting in a disorganized formation. The enemy seized the opportunity to strike, and the situation drastically changed. Xu Zhuo, the left forward of the "Bomber" team, repeatedly made successful shots, gaining great prestige. The score difference was 15-5. In total, the "Bomber" team won the God Group championship of this tournament with a final score of 23-16. The referee was Gong Zhenyi.

World-Renowned Track and Field Athlete Kinue Hitomi Retires 129

(Tokyo Dispatch) Kinue Hitomi, a world-renowned Japanese track and field athlete, is now 25 years old. In 1927, she attended the Second World Women's Games at the age of only 19. Fighting alone, she broke four world records, instantly stunning the world. She is a talented track and field athlete. Her records in the 60-meter dash (7.4 seconds), 100-meter dash (12 seconds), and long jump (6.07 meters) remain unbroken to this day. Her 100-meter result once reached 11.8 seconds, and her name is known worldwide. However, when she participated in the Third World Women's Games last year, her performance declined. She finished third in the 60-meter dash and javelin throw. In the long jump, she won again with a result of 5.95 meters, but she still finished second in the individual overall score. Since returning to Japan, she has been quite discouraged and has been giving speeches everywhere without rest, leading to a severe case of pleurisy. She was hospitalized in Osaka Medical University Hospital last October. She has been seriously ill several times, and doctors were particularly worried. She barely survived, but she has been bedridden for more than half a year and has not yet recovered. Her vitality has been greatly diminished. She knows that the World Games to be held next year in Los Angeles, USA, are approaching, but her life is in danger. She shed tears of sadness and announced her departure from track and field life, retiring from competition. The entire nation of Japan is deeply saddened by this.

Page 16

National Jinan University 4th Anniversary of University Establishment & 25th Anniversary of School Founding Special Issue No. 1

Preface 130

— Li Bangdong

Today marks the 25th anniversary of our school's founding and the fourth anniversary of its expansion into a university. It is also the graduation ceremony, and the anniversary of President Zheng's return to the school four years ago. Our school colleagues are filled with celebration and joy, and we are honored to have members of the community join us for this grand occasion. Last night, Director Fan advocated for an advance celebration, like a birthday celebration. Today, the atmosphere within the school is vibrant, and our spirits are indescribably joyful. Regarding the school's past achievements, from middle school to a single-faculty university, and then expanded into a comprehensive university by President Zheng, this publication contains detailed accounts, so I will not elaborate further. I am mindful of Jinan's position and the great mission it bears, as well as its rapid progress in recent years. Today's grand event is indeed unlike any ordinary anniversary, and it is more worthy of celebration and praise than any other academic institution. As I participate in this grand occasion, I believe that our school's anniversary today contains at least three essential meanings:

1. Promoting Public Awareness of Jinan

I recall in the winter of 1928 when I accompanied President Zheng to the north to welcome the coffin. In the past, President Zheng governed the northern region, and his benevolence was widely praised. Former colleagues all came to pay their respects. Some, hearing that our president was now in charge of Jinan, even asked about the location of the school. I was very surprised and secretly regretted why Jinan's name was not known to everyone. Upon reflection, it was not surprising. In the past, Jinan was solely dedicated to cultivating the children of overseas Chinese, with little contact with people in the country, resulting in a sense of separation. Since President Zheng's return, he first expanded the scope of education, broadened its purpose, not only to nurture the children of overseas Chinese but also to cultivate outstanding domestic youth who would help the overseas Chinese develop their businesses, exchanging cultures, and focusing on the big picture. What has been the impact on domestic society over the past four years? How does the broad Jinan of today compare to the narrow Jinan of the past in terms of achievements and mission? The opening of this grand event is precisely to promote a definite understanding of Jinan among the public.

2. Enhancing Jinan's Academic Standing Internationally

The academic and cultural progress of a nation must be represented by its leading academic institutions, showcasing it to the world. Examples include Cambridge and Oxford in England, Harvard and Yale in America, Paris in France, and Leuven in Belgium. We all know their significance. Then, which academic institution in our country can represent the civilization of this great Eastern nation and be respected by the world? We dare not presume to make false claims. However, given Jinan's short history, with students coming from overseas and talents cultivated and returned to their respective countries, all interacting and engaging with people from foreign lands, its relationship with the international community and its level of civilization can represent our nation. Today's event includes an achievement exhibition, inspiring a sense of awe. How should we promote Jinan's academic culture to elevate its international standing in the future?

3. Advancing the Substantive Content of the Only Overseas Chinese University

Jinan has been in existence for 25 years, enduring various crises and setbacks. It was also interrupted due to political turmoil. It has only been four years since its expansion into a university. The school funds are stretched thin, and maintaining regular operations is already difficult. Special equipment has not been improved at all. It is thanks to President Zheng's skillful management that the school's property has been used to maintain operations, which is commendable. He once said, "I would rather endure hardship and build the school on a solid foundation, and then seek support from others to further its development, rather than deceive people with empty words and seek help blindly." Therefore, Jinan is reluctant to solicit donations from elders at home and abroad easily. However, the student tuition is the lowest among national universities. The school has achieved today's results through economic methods. On this double anniversary, as we review the past and look forward to the future, how should we promote this only overseas Chinese university to make its content more substantial? Regarding concerns, there is no shortage of enlightened and enthusiastic individuals at home and abroad. In the future, they might also be happy to support Jinan to share President Zheng's responsibility.

From this perspective, Jinan's achievements today are due to President Zheng's tireless efforts. A great harvest comes from distant causes. Jinan's unique spirit was established from the beginning of the school's founding. Please read the school song handwritten by President Zheng during the founding of the school, which reveals that it has a origin and is not accidental. I respectfully record it at the end of my article, using it as a preface. The song goes:

Colonization in Java, our ancestors pioneered, tracing back to ancient times. Why are the elders sleeping soundly, letting others take the lead?

Having cultivated the land with Europeans, we also suffer from harsh taxes. Alas, my compatriots have fallen into the abyss, when will we see the light?

A true man will never accept pity, but instead, pay taxes diligently. Superiority and inferiority are the laws of nature, so let's study science well.

Swearing to expand our country's maritime power, this great responsibility rests on our shoulders. Awaken the spirit of overseas Chinese, and the situation will change. The beautiful rivers and mountains are waiting.

Photo of President Zheng When He First Took Office as Head of the School in the 34th Year of the Guangxu Emperor's Reign 132

Commemorative Words 133

— Zheng Hongnian

I participated in the founding of Jinan School in the thirty-third year of the Qing Guangxu reign, and I reassumed the post of President of Jinan University in the summer of the sixteenth year of the Republic of China. Counting from the former, it has been twenty-five years to this day; counting from the latter, it has also been four years since the reorganization. Alas! Overseas Chinese education is the pivotal point for the rise and fall of our Chinese nation, and the lifeline for the fate of hundreds of millions of overseas Chinese compatriots. It is certainly no small matter concerning one dynasty, one region, or one person! Regardless of my limited abilities, I followed in the footsteps of the late Premier Sun, continuing his unfinished grand vision, and shouldered this heavy responsibility to this day. Now, on the occasion of the twenty-fifth anniversary, I do not forget the past and respectfully recount one or two things to inform the people of the country.

Recalling the establishment of Jinan School, it was not initially a predetermined plan. At that time, Mr. Qian Nianqiu, the Minister to the Netherlands, sent a counselor to investigate the educational situation in Java, deeply concerned that overseas Chinese children did not know about their ancestral culture and feared the extinction of their race. He then telegraphed Liangjiang Governor-General Duan Fang, requesting him to find a place for returning overseas Chinese students to study. At the beginning of receiving the telegram, Governor-General Duan did not even know what Java meant. It was only after replying to the telegram that he learned Java was a Dutch colony, and that twenty-one overseas Chinese students would return to the country for study. After receiving approval from the Qing court, Mr. Dong Hongyi escorted them north. As most of the overseas Chinese students were registered under the provinces of Fujian and Guangdong, I and Mr. Wen Bingzhong were assigned to take charge of the matter. Mr. Chen Botao, the Jiangnan Director of Studies, strongly supported this initiative and even established a school for lectures, naming it "Jinan." Speaking of the national situation, Nanyang had long been a battleground for the world's great powers, and overseas Chinese had long suffered the pain of being butchered and slaughtered like fish and meat. The establishment of Jinan School was already late. However, those in positions of authority were ignorant and oblivious to the great trends of the world. Governor-General Duan's establishment of Jinan School was even listed in impeachments by those in power. When Zhang Xun stationed troops in Jiangning, Jinan School was placed under strict surveillance. At that time, the people of our country were so isolated from the overseas Chinese situation.

However, the ardent patriotism of the overseas Chinese students was evident from the very beginning of the school. Jinan School was founded the year after the late Premier Sun organized the Tongmenghui (Revolutionary Alliance). The school song I composed at that time focused on awakening national consciousness, which coincided with the Premier's revolutionary goals. Therefore, revolutionary ideas among the students were greatly developed. Around the time of the Xinhai Revolution, some students went to Baoding Military Academy, and others went to study naval affairs. After the revolution began, some went to Wuhan, and some went to Shanghai, all with the ambition to dedicate themselves to serving the country. I still remember that overseas Chinese student, Li Quanfa, was the youngest. One day, he said to me, "Nanyang is the Nanyang of our Chinese nation. Shouldn't those with ambition seek to expand southward!" Although his words were straightforward, his heroic spirit could penetrate the sun and moon! Modern scholars say that the newly emerging people's spirit is full of vigor, and the overseas Chinese students possessed it!

During the Xinhai Revolution, the overseas Chinese students dispersed, and Jinan School was suspended. It was not until the sixth year of the Republic of China that, with the efforts of Mr. Huang Yanpei, preparations were made to reopen the school. In the seventh year of the Republic of China, Jinan School reopened. Since then, Jinan School has been advancing with twists and turns. Mr. Zhao Zhengping served as president from the seventh year of the Republic of China until his resignation in the fourteenth year of the Republic of China, serving a total of seven years. (During the tenth year of the Republic of China, Mr. Ke Zhenxin served as president for one year.) The expansion of the normal school and business school, the completion of the junior high school department, the addition of the business school university department, the purchase of land for the school, and the construction of school buildings were all planned and managed by Mr. Zhengping. In the autumn of the fourteenth year of the Republic of China, Mr. Jiang Bohan succeeded as president, and the organization of the business school university department was largely finalized. Moreover, during times of successive turmoil, Jinan School was able to be maintained without declining due to the efforts of Mr. Bohan and the various school board members. In the summer of the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, I was ordered to take over Jinan School and subsequently received the appointment as president. As an old man, I reassumed the presidency of Jinan University. Speaking personally, overseas Chinese education has been an unfinished wish for the past twenty years, and fulfilling this duty is to fulfill that wish. Speaking publicly, the Premier took rescuing overseas Chinese compatriots as one of the goals of the national revolution, and enhancing education and culture for overseas Chinese is to repay the Premier.

When I first received the order, I immediately expanded the organization and reorganized it into a complete university. In addition to the business school, departments of Chinese Language and Literature, Foreign Languages and Literature, Educational Psychology, Mathematics and Physics, Law, Biology, and History and Sociology were established one after another, and the scale was roughly determined. It is difficult and arduous to start anything, and this is especially true for education. At that time, the lack of talent and the simplicity of materials were all obstacles to expanding the organization. I then visited and sought out famous Confucian scholars and great academics to preside over the lectures; respected the etiquette of teachers and advocated a style of good learning. All that was necessary to gather talents and create a university, I exhausted my heart and diligently sought it. As for the construction of material facilities, the library was completed in the autumn of the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, and the Lientao Hall was built in the winter. The following year, the Science Hall was built first, followed by the junior high school dormitory and classrooms. By the nineteenth year of the Republic of China, the Zhiyuan Hall and the high school dormitory, as well as the middle school department office, were built one after another, and the project was not far from my predetermined plan. Raising tens of thousands of huge sums and managing dozens of construction projects, my heart and energy have also been exhausted!

Currently, the organization of the university includes five colleges: the College of Liberal Arts, the College of Science, the College of Law, the College of Education, and the College of Business. The middle school department includes five departments: the General Studies Department, the Normal School Department, the Business Department, the Agricultural Department, and the Junior High School. In addition, there are four departments: the Secretariat, the Student Affairs Office, the Hongnian Library, and the Nanyang and American Cultural Affairs Department, each responsible for their duties, complementing the academic affairs. In recent years, the ideological circles have been empty, superficial, and shallow, and young students have been superficial and fleeting, which is truly worrying. I am striving to correct this shortcoming. The university's specialized departments are divided into specialized fields to cultivate a style of specialized academic research. Various schools of thought, those that do not conflict with each other, are open to students for free research, but only with the aim of in-depth study and not pursuing empty fame. In recent years, social customs have been thin, and the trend of personal self-interest has increased. All the dirty deeds of petty gains and dog fights are openly adorned with beautiful words, and they live in them without shame. The old ethics have been destroyed, and the new ethics have no discipline. The degradation of human nature to that of animals is chilling. I am striving to punish this shortcoming, taking ethics as the first priority of human discipline; in school, we respect the way of teachers; at home, we cultivate family friendship; in society, we uphold justice; and in the country, we maintain public loyalty. We hope that today's good young people will be tomorrow's good citizens. In recent years, factionalism and partisanship have been everywhere, and the education community, which prides itself on being noble, is also in the same dirty state. In the past few years, I have been fighting against the so-called factions alone. They respond to me with selfishness, and I respond with public interest. Those who wanted to take Jinan University to plant their power eventually returned in vain. In the past, there were often trends formed by waves, but now teachers and students are at peace with each other, with no differences, and purely tending towards academic competition. Secondary education is based on strict training. The curriculum emphasizes basic practice and also emphasizes vocational guidance. Moral training is taken for ideological education to cultivate a complete personality. Middle school is the foundation of the university, and middle school students are the backbone of society, which is the so-called basic education. If middle school students are dissolute and unruly and their tools are not well-trained, it is difficult to glimpse the hall of learning. If their behavior is not restrained, it is difficult to endure the hardships of adversity. The so-called jade must be carved before it can become a useful object. Moreover, overseas Chinese students are naturally candid and their emotions are easily impulsive. Letting them go will lead to rudeness, and pruning and managing them can make them talented. This is why I advocate strict training. As for the patriotism of overseas Chinese students, which flows into extremism, I mainly guide them. Overseas Chinese students return to the country from thousands of miles away, escaping from the iron fist of imperialism under heavy pressure. Their breathing is initially relieved, and their feelings are often deep. They suffer from unequal treatment between ethnic groups and cherish their homeland, and their desire for governance is even more urgent. Moreover, our school's students are all children of middle-class families and below, and they are familiar with the suffering of the people. They take the rise and fall of their families and countries as their own responsibility. Those who preside over education should not hinder this vigor. The way to guide them is to make young people turn to pragmatism, either studying literature, science, or sports, each mastering a skill and each studying a subject. By approaching it with vigor, they can make progress endlessly. Our school's sports, regardless of university or middle school, develop evenly. Without promotion, the technology is improving day by day, which is proof of this. Students' extracurricular study is assisted by the library and research room. The library has more than 100,000 volumes of Chinese and Western books, and the annual book fee is 6,000 yuan as usual. Research rooms are set up in colleges and departments, with professors as mentors. Students each study their own subjects and conduct special research. The research results are compiled and published in quarterly journals for the academic community. The Nanyang and American Cultural Affairs Department is responsible for the research on Nanyang culture, publishing Nanyang Research and Nanyang Series to promote the attention of the Chinese people, and issuing Nanyang Newsletter to disseminate domestic news. Important issues in Nanyang are specially treated by the staff of the department, and they are written into papers for the reference of overseas Chinese compatriots. As for the guidance of returning overseas Chinese students and the supervision of overseas Chinese students in the school, the Student Affairs Office is responsible for it; the Secretariat is responsible for the receipt and expenditure of government affairs and the management of general affairs. Our school's finances are completely open, and even the smallest amount of money can be audited. This is the policy that I have followed since I became the president of the school, and it is what the staff of each session has adhered to.

As I said earlier, overseas Chinese education is no small matter concerning one dynasty, one region, or one person. I have exhausted my foolishness, but I sigh that I cannot reach the depths! Education is to adapt to the needs of society; what overseas Chinese compatriots expect from our Jinan University is to cultivate talents specialized in industry and commerce, and teachers for overseas Chinese education. How many have been trained in the past twenty-five years? What overseas Chinese compatriots expect from our Jinan University is a practical reform plan for industry and commerce, and an improvement plan for economic policies. How much has been planned for overseas Chinese compatriots in the past twenty-five years? Not only that, but overseas Chinese schools rely on the breath of foreigners and let them live and die on their own. Our Jinan University has not planned a policy of protection. Hundreds of thousands of overseas Chinese children who are out of school are allowed to win or lose and return to natural evolution. Our Jinan University has not planned a rescue plan. Those who are engaged in overseas Chinese education, our Jinan University has not tried its best to nurture them, and they are uneven. Moreover, due to the different times of development in various parts of Nanyang, the age of receiving education is very different. Our Jinan University has not been able to consider this fact and make up for it separately. Overseas Chinese students are all under strict management overseas, and their parents and brothers are also strictly supervising them. When they return to the country from thousands of miles away, they are far away from their parents and brothers. Our Jinan University has not been able to fulfill the responsibility of parents and teachers, and they sometimes fall into indulgence. Most of the overseas Chinese students are children of poor families, and those who are talented are in poverty. Our Jinan University has not been able to raise enough funds to support these talents. In the end, Jinan University claims to be an overseas Chinese education, but it is no different from other schools. This is what I worry about day and night! Alas! If the national spirit is not revitalized for one day, the national fortune of China will not have the hope of prosperity for one day. If the Chinese nation is not revived for one day, the weak and small nations will not have the chance of recovery for one day. If the Nanyang problem is not resolved for one day, world peace will not have the possibility of realization for one day! I dedicate my aging body to Jinan University, which is to dedicate myself to overseas Chinese education; to repay the Premier, which is to repay the country. Compatriots, overseas Chinese compatriots! Teachers and students of our Jinan University, many hands make light work. Strive for this one breath for the Chinese nation, and perhaps we can compete with the great powers!

President Zheng Hongnian 134
