Review and Outlook of Jinan University 136

— Fan Shouzhi

(I)

Jinan University was born in the thirty-third year of Qing Guangxu (1907), and this year marks its twenty-fifth anniversary. Jinan University is a school that bears the special mission of "Overseas Chinese Education." Its life is closely related to the lives of millions of overseas Chinese, and its history is a reflection of the life history of overseas Chinese. In this important sense, we should look back at the evolution of the past twenty-five years.

In the late Qing Dynasty, the atmosphere of "National Awakening" was very strong. Premier Sun's revolutionary cause was most diligently awakening the national consciousness at that time. At the same time, the capitalist sphere of influence expanded to the Pacific, and the Nanyang Islands became a battleground for imperialists. Overseas Chinese compatriots lived under the eaves of others and felt the oppression of imperialists at the outset. Therefore, overseas Chinese compatriots recognized Premier Sun's revolutionary cause the earliest and supported it the most. Jinan School was born in this pervasive atmosphere of national awakening.

The first person to pay attention to overseas Chinese education was Mr. Qian Nianqiu, the Minister to the Netherlands. He understood the crisis of the Chinese nation in the international arena and telegraphed Liangjiang Governor-General Duan Fang, asking him to plan a place for overseas Chinese students to study in the country. Governor-General Duan obtained the permission of the Qing court and invited the current President Zheng Hongnian and Mr. Wen Bingzhong to preside over this matter. The first group of overseas Chinese students who returned to the country were all from Java, totaling twenty-three. Later, places such as Bama Long, Jian Yili, Baca, and Surabaya successively sent some overseas Chinese students back to the country. In the winter of the second year of its founding, there were already 115 overseas Chinese students. In two years, the number of overseas Chinese students increased so quickly, which shows that overseas Chinese compatriots' longing for the motherland was very enthusiastic. Among the overseas Chinese students, they all eagerly expected the revival of China. They not only sympathized with the national revolution but also plucked up the courage to participate. At that time, Jinan School in Nanjing became the center of the revolution. President Zheng did his best to protect the revolutionary cause. The school song he made had the sentence "Pledge to expand the sea power of the motherland, the great task is on our shoulders; awaken the overseas Chinese soul and change the situation, beautiful mountains and rivers," which boiled the blood of many young people!

However, this patriotic enthusiasm interrupted the life of Jinan. The Qing court said a lot of gossip about Governor-General Duan's establishment of Jinan School to accommodate revolutionary youths. The General of Jiangning even used Manchu teachers to monitor Jinan School. Zhang Xun stationed troops in Nanjing and regarded overseas Chinese students without braids as extremely rebellious. In the third year of Xuantong, the revolutionary army launched an uprising in Wuchang, and the provinces in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River responded one after another. Overseas Chinese students in Jinan could not bear this stifling atmosphere and went to Wuchang and Shanghai to participate in revolutionary work, so Jinan School was dissolved invisibly.

Secretary-General Mr. Fan Shouzhi 137

(II)

The reopening of Jinan School was in the seventh year of the Republic of China. President Zheng deeply regretted the suspension of Jinan School and tried several times to find a way to reopen it, but he never succeeded. Because Yuan Shikai was afraid that overseas Chinese students would engage in revolution and that overseas Chinese students would help Premier Sun, the reopening of Jinan was hopeless during his lifetime. After the failure of Hongxian's imperial regime and the death of Yuan Shikai, Mr. Huang Yanpei traveled around and began preparations in the winter of the sixth year of the Republic of China, and it was officially established in the spring of the seventh year of the Republic of China, with Zhao Zhengping as the president. At that time, the European War was raging, and white people were busy fighting each other, so they had no time to look east. The industry and commerce of the Nanyang Islands rose in this opportunity. The revived Jinan School met the needs of this environment: first, to cultivate some commercial talents for overseas Chinese compatriots, and second, to cultivate some teachers for overseas Chinese schools for overseas Chinese compatriots. Mr. Zhao Zhengping served as president for seven years and paid the most attention to the Normal School Department and the Business Department, and the equipment was the most complete. Later, he also added the Business School University Department.

The relocation of the school site from Nanjing to Zhenru was also Mr. Zhao Zhengping's plan. He believed that revitalizing commerce was the only way for overseas Chinese compatriots to save themselves, so he worked hard to cultivate commercial experts. The relocation of the school site to near Shanghai was intended to make students close to modern cities and give students the opportunity to practice. Unfortunately, the school building was just completed in the thirteenth year of the Republic of China, and the war in Jiangsu and Zhejiang broke out. The original students of the Business School University Department had to borrow studies from China Public School, not to mention any expansion.

After the fourteenth year of the Republic of China, Mr. Jiang Bohan successively served as president for two years. In the changing situation, he barely completed the organization of the Business School University Department and enriched the high school liberal arts department, normal school department, business department, and junior high school department. After the European War, overseas Chinese compatriots were able to maintain their commercial status temporarily, and many overseas Chinese students returned to the country in those years. In the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, the number of students increased to more than 700. Then came the great tide of the National Revolution. In the spring of the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, the National Revolutionary Army occupied Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and Jinan School was expanded into a complete university by President Zheng.

(III)

President Zheng's ambition to reassume the presidency was very grand. He wanted to stabilize the foundation of Jinan University, devote himself to overseas Chinese education to repay Premier Sun, and build a pure academic research institution to comfort the expectations of overseas Chinese elders. Overseas Chinese compatriots are scattered everywhere, with a total of more than six million. Calculated by a thousandth ratio, there are at least tens of thousands of overseas Chinese students. The original buildings of Jinan School can accommodate up to 500 people, which is materially insufficient. In the past four years, President Zheng has tried his best to plan material construction, and has successively built Lientao Hall, Science Hall, Auditorium, Junior High School Dormitory, High School Dormitory, Girls' Dormitory, Faculty and Staff Dormitory, Faculty and Staff Residences, Middle School Department Office, and Middle School Department Classrooms, totaling more than ten items. According to the current situation, it can accommodate 1,500 people. As for books, instruments, and sports equipment, etc., they are added every year, close to 100,000 yuan. Jinan University is in a pioneering situation. Without this massive material construction, the foundation would be difficult to stabilize, and President Zheng took on this responsibility.

Premier Sun's revolutionary cause benefited greatly from the help of overseas Chinese compatriots, so the Premier always cared about the well-being of overseas Chinese compatriots throughout his life and was determined to rescue overseas Chinese compatriots from the unequal iron fist. However, the revolutionary cause has not yet been completed, and Premier Sun has unfortunately passed away. The wish to repay overseas Chinese compatriots has not been achieved. President Zheng took over Jinan University to inherit Premier Sun's wish. President Zheng said: "I am willing to dedicate myself to running overseas Chinese education well, so that overseas Chinese elders can restore their inherent national spirit, and I can also be worthy of the late Premier and comfort his spirit in heaven." In these four years, although President Zheng has not been able to live in the school often because he has been serving the country, his mind has always been planning everything for Jinan.

President Zheng's policy of running Jinan University is to make Jinan University a pure academic research institution. He said: "Saving the country cannot be done by empty shouts. The only way to save the country is to bury oneself in academic research." Since the establishment of the National Government, political tutelage has begun. A country like China, which is vast and rich in resources, lacks nothing but academic experts. After the May Fourth Movement, students were called from schools to the streets, and the streets were full of patriotic youths. Now everyone should be aware that they should return from the streets to the research room. In the past four years, President Zheng has solemnly raised the words "Saving the country through academic research" in every speech, and pointed out the world economic crisis after 1928 and the trend of economic bankruptcy of overseas Chinese, using it to prove that overseas Chinese students' academic research is the great way for overseas Chinese to save themselves. Now, the five colleges of the Faculty, the College of Education, the College of Science, the College of Law, and the College of Business, and the five departments of the Middle School Department, the General Science Department, the Normal School Department, the Business Department, the Agriculture Department, and the Junior High School, have all been fully established. The professors and teachers of each department are recruited from all over the country by President Zheng with the aim of concentrating talents, and they are working together under the banner of academic research.

(IV)

The anniversary is approaching, and we look back at the past. These twenty-five years have completed three tasks: A. In the national awakening movement, aroused the overseas Chinese compatriots' understanding of the motherland; B. Cultivated many commercial and educational experts in the economic revival of overseas Chinese; C. Established a century-old foundation for overseas Chinese education and expanded Jinan University into a complete academic research university. We look to the future again, and there are many places that should be worked hard for the important mission of "Overseas Chinese Education".

President Zheng said: "I came to run Jinan University to soothe my conscience. I do not use Jinan as a tool for myself or for my personal rights. Everyone should support Jinan, not me personally." Everyone should support Jinan; this is a fundamental statement. All undertakings are built bit by bit by hundreds or thousands of people. President Zheng has exhausted his efforts in material construction and organizational expansion. How to continue this undertaking and how to expand it further is everyone's responsibility. In terms of material construction, important buildings such as the gymnasium, museum, and dining hall are in President Zheng's planned projects, so I will not mention them for now. It is extremely common for a university's library to store tens of millions of books and for a science museum to have tens of millions of dollars' worth of experimental equipment. We, Jinan University, still feel that we are far from this standard. It is also extremely common for a university's academic research to produce a powerful school of thought, such as the French Academy, the Paris Faculty of Arts, the École Normale Supérieure, and the École des Chartes, each representing a school of thought in history. Although our Jinan University aims at overseas Chinese education, there are still very few achievements in specialized research. The Nanyang Islands are proving grounds for various specialized academic disciplines. In addition to teaching returning overseas Chinese students, our Jinan University should also conduct separate investigations into Nanyang, which can be used for specialized academic studies. We have already made a start on the academic research direction proposed by President Zheng. We must carry the heavy burden and walk step by step from today onwards towards that distant future!

The hardships experienced by overseas Chinese in Nanyang in recent years can be said to be the most difficult in the past century, but in the near future, there is no possibility of escaping these hardships. Since Jinan University is closely related to the lives of overseas Chinese, we should find a way to help our compatriots escape their suffering. Moreover, if a world war breaks out, the overseas Chinese in the Nanyang Islands, which are in the sphere of influence of the United Kingdom, Japan, and the United States, will experience even more difficult hardships. We should also plan for how to prevent and relieve these hardships for our compatriots. This is a major responsibility at present, and we must all shoulder it together!

In short, twenty-five years is a very short period, and we have done very little with all our efforts! President Zheng has twice devoted his efforts to overseas Chinese education, and we should work together to continue his undertaking! Let us not forget "saving the country through scholarship," and let us not forget to support Jinan. Only then can we fulfill the mission of overseas Chinese education!

Xiong Shihui's Speech on the Spreading Disaster in Jiangxi 142

Saving the Disaster Victims in Jiangxi

Is Saving China

Is Saving Everyone Themselves

Xiong Shihui, Commander of the Songhu Garrison, held a reception for people from all walks of life at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce last night regarding the Jiangxi disaster relief effort. Xu Shiying, Wang Yiting, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Shi Liangcai, Wang Boqi, and several hundred others attended. Xiong delivered a speech, stating that the severity of the disaster in Jiangxi is a hundred times greater than the drought in the Northwest and the floods in the Northeast. This is well known. As for the Jiangxi disaster relief effort, I have held receptions for people from all walks of life several times. I hope that the people of the country will not say that I am particularly enthusiastic about my hometown. I am indeed from Jiangxi, but the disaster in Jiangxi is by no means a problem for Jiangxi Province alone. Because the bandit disaster in Jiangxi is spreading, if relief is not provided urgently, it will spread to neighboring provinces and become widespread throughout the country, even more terrible than the influenza epidemic that spread to Shanghai years ago. As you all know, the Jiangxi bandits who kill and set fires target the general population, especially those over thirty years of age, those with more than five hundred yuan in property, or the educated intellectuals. As long as one of these three conditions is met, they will be slaughtered. Today, all of you present probably possess the above three qualifications. From the bandits' point of view, you are all on the list for slaughter. Now, if we do not provide relief to the people of Jiangxi who have suffered from the bandit disaster, the bandits will become even more numerous in the future. When the whole country is filled with bandits, not only will we be unable to help others, but I am afraid that there will be no one to save us. Therefore, saving Jiangxi is saving China, and saving the disaster victims in Jiangxi is saving everyone themselves. All circles in Shanghai have already raised huge sums for the droughts in the Northwest and the floods in the Northeast. I believe that they will be even more enthusiastic in providing assistance to the bandit disaster in Jiangxi, which is a hundred times more harmful. Xu Shiying then spoke, saying that the natural disasters in the Northwest and Northeast can be seen and heard. As long as there is money, the dead can be buried, the cold can be clothed, and the hungry can be fed. The human disaster in Jiangxi has resulted in the slaughter of hundreds of thousands of people, the starvation and freezing to death of hundreds of thousands of people, and the displacement of millions of people with nowhere to return. Not only can it not be seen, but even the exact number cannot be investigated. If relief is not provided urgently, more people will be forced to become bandits in the future. We must first save Jiangxi before we can talk about saving China. Yu Qiaqing then spoke, saying that the Jiangxi bandit problem is a matter of national survival and the life and death of the nation, which is more important than any other problem. If the Jiangxi problem can be resolved, the Guangdong problem need not be worried about. Therefore, we must all do our best to help. Wang Xiaolai then spoke, saying that although we in Shanghai have already written many donation checks, we ultimately hope that we in Shanghai can save others, and do not want others to come to Shanghai to save us. Moreover, Commander Xiong is the most wise commander Shanghai has ever had. Our various groups have already raised more than 180,000 yuan for the drought in Shaanxi. We should be even more enthusiastic in donating to the Jiangxi disaster relief effort advocated by Commander Xiong.

Obligation is Absolute, Not a Right

Since the central military plan decided to focus all efforts on suppressing bandits in Jiangxi Province, Commander Xiong was summoned to stay in Beijing for many days. He plans to recruit talents from all parties to conduct in-depth research and formulate plans for implementation. Those from Jiangxi who have special talents and can contribute to various issues, regardless of their previous history in the province, are all among those to be recruited. The wise should exert their abilities, the rich should contribute their wealth, the elders should supervise education, and farmers and workers should resume their work. Everyone must be united, and all actions must be carried out in accordance with military law. Only then, after the military has achieved a degree of success, will the common disaster be immediately cleared. What is particularly important is that our common purpose in going to Jiangxi this time is entirely driven by the obligation to love our hometown. We must sacrifice everything, strive to be the government's backing, and seek to enrich our self-reliance, without any private plans for rights. All colleagues must unanimously recognize this. According to this prediction, when Commander-in-Chief Chiang sets off, the accompanying commissioners will be very numerous.

Zhang Ji Passes Through Shanghai to Go to Beijing 144

Hoping that the Guangdong Issue Can Still Be Resolved Peacefully

Currently Researching Appropriate Solutions

Going to Beijing Tonight to Report on the Progress

Zhang Ji, a member of the Central Supervisory Committee, was ordered to go to Guangdong to mediate for peace. He arrived in Shanghai on the President Wilson from Hong Kong on the 11th. He arrived at the port at 10:30 AM yesterday morning. Liu Luyin, Minister of the Central Propaganda Department, and Chen Xizeng, Director of the Public Security Bureau, personally welcomed him at the pier. After Zhang landed, he went with Liu to Wu Tiecheng's residence on Haig Road to rest. He will take the night express train to Beijing at 11:45 PM tonight to attend the Fifth Plenary Session, report on the progress of negotiations in Guangdong, and discuss the corresponding policy. The situation of his arrival at the port yesterday and Zhang's remarks are recorded below.

The Ship Docks at the Huangpu River: The President Wilson docked at the Fifteenth Pontoon on the Huangpu River at 10:30 AM yesterday morning, near Yangshupu Lan Road. Liu Luyin, Minister of the Central Propaganda Department, and reporters from various newspapers took the Dala Company's small boat from the New Customs Wharf to welcome him. Chen Xizeng, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, took another Maochang Company's small boat with more than ten police officers to welcome him. They all boarded the ship to meet with Zhang. Zhang was wearing a white linen long gown and smiled as he shook hands with the welcomers, saying that the heat in Guangdong was unbearable and the northerners found it very uncomfortable. He then took the Maochang small boat with Liu and others to the New Customs Wharf to land at 11:10 AM. He then took a car with Liu to Wu Tiecheng's residence to rest.

Hope for Peace: After meeting with Zhang on the ship, this newspaper's reporter had a long conversation with him on the way back on the Maochang small boat. Zhang said that he had repeatedly contacted Mr. Tang Shaochuan, Sun Zhesheng, Wang Zhaoming, and Gu Xiangqin in Guangdong. Both sides were eager for peace, and what they were eager to resolve was the method of peace. This trip to Beijing to attend the Fifth Plenary Session is to report on the attitude of the Guangdong side and to discuss an appropriate solution. I firmly believe that it will not resort to force.

No Comment: When the reporter asked about the two methods of mediation that were rumored to have been drafted by the Central Committee members in Shanghai, (1) holding a plenary meeting of the Central Supervisory Committee in Shanghai, and (2) establishing a political branch in Guangdong, and asked what the Guangdong side's response was to this, Zhang made no comment. He only said that both sides were comrades of many years, and there was nothing that could not be discussed. After arriving in Beijing, I will meet with the various committees and then discuss it.

The Premier's Hometown: Zhang also said that I once accompanied Mr. Tang Shaochuan to visit Zhongshan County, stayed for six days, admired the Premier's residence in Cuiheng Village, and visited the construction projects in Zhongshan County. The progress of all matters was very admirable. The county magistrate is still concurrently held by Tang. The houses in the Premier's ancestral village all face east, but the Premier's house alone faces west, which is also a unique point.

Secretaries Stay in Guangdong: Zhang's two secretaries, Huang Jianfen and Sheng Cheng, who accompanied him to Guangdong, were once kidnapped by bandits in Guangdong. According to Zhang, they were kidnapped by bandits while playing at Baiyun Temple. The authorities ordered Panyu County to solve the case within three days. The bandits knew that the county government was looking for them, so they sent them out the next day. They are now out of danger and are recuperating in Guangzhou due to minor illnesses. They will return to Shanghai soon.

Not Going North for the Time Being: Zhang also said that everyone in the country, from top to bottom, hopes for peace, and only the Communist Party and certain foreigners do not want our country to be in chaos. For example, the recent rumors that I will stay in Guangdong and not return, and that I will return north from Hong Kong instead of going to Nanjing, are all kinds of discord and instigation, and their joy in chaos is obvious. This time I am going to Beijing to discuss mediation methods with the Central Government and will not go north for the time being.

Telegram to Beijing: After arriving in Shanghai, Zhang immediately telegraphed Beijing through Chen Xizeng to report his whereabouts, and said that he would take the night train to Beijing tonight to personally report everything.

Visit to Zhang Jingjiang: After lunch at Wu's residence yesterday afternoon, Zhang went with Liu Luyin to Masnan Road at 1:30 PM to visit Zhang Jingjiang, report on the progress of the negotiations, and talk in detail for about half an hour before leaving. Zhang Jingjiang is temporarily unable to go to Beijing due to illness.

Unresolved Case of National Products Department Store Closure 154

The Municipal Council Says Equipment is Fully Restorable

Staff Posting Slogans Arrested then Released

The Chinese National Products United Department Store has remained closed for five days since the Shanghai Municipal Council ordered its shutdown. The following is a record of yesterday's events:

Industrial Department Investigation: Guo Bingwen, Director of the Industrial and Commercial Affairs Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, was ordered by the ministry to investigate the closure of the Chinese National Products United Department Store by the Municipal Council. Yesterday, he specially dispatched Pan Zengyin to investigate the truth from all sides in order to report back to the ministry.

Municipal Council Letter: Michael, Acting Secretary of the Public Concession Municipal Council, sent a letter to the National Products Department Store yesterday, saying, "To Mr. Zhang Deyin of the National Products Department Store: Regarding your letter of June 4th to the assistant of the Revenue Department of our bureau, discussing the improvements the Municipal Council and the Fire Brigade require before issuing a license to your store, we now reply to you that while some improvements have been made, conversely, our bureau believes that many of your store's imperfect facilities actually reduce the safety of the building. The improvements required by our departments are purely for the sake of protecting the lives and property of the people within the concession. If you can comply with these requirements and they are deemed satisfactory by the relevant departments, the license to resume business can be issued immediately. We hope for your cooperation."

Staff Arrested and Released: Staff members of the National Products Department Store have been arrested by the police three times, and all have been released completely. Yesterday morning at 4:40 AM, two staff members, Lou Shangde, a clerk from Shuntai Silk Store, and Jiang Sibao, a new staff member from Sanlin Toys, were arrested by Chinese detectives from the New Gate Police Station for posting slogans. They were detained for two hours and then released.

Party Headquarters Instructions: Wu Kaixian, Pan Gongzhan, and Wu Bochen, standing committee members of the Municipal Party Headquarters, received a petition yesterday from the National Products Department Store regarding the unwarranted closure of the Chinese National Products United Department Store by the Public Concession Police, requesting serious negotiations. The instructions given were to forward the petition to the Municipal Government for review with additional comments.

Manufacturer's Petition: The National Products Department Store Manufacturers Association sent a letter to Wu Jingxiong and He Deqiu, municipal advisors to the Municipal Council, stating, "To Mr. Deqiu and Mr. Jingxiong: We, the manufacturers, recognizing the weakness of national products and the failure of vigorous promotion, participated in the National Products Department Store in July of last year at the former Municipal Hall site on Nanjing Road, aiming to promote sales and develop the future. However, since participating, the progress has been extremely difficult due to the embryonic stage of national products. Statistics show that annual losses have exceeded one million. We have not allowed such a large sacrifice to hinder our initial purpose. This time, the department store moved to the historically significant New World site in Shanghai for reorganization, hoping to develop the business after initial planning. Unexpectedly, on the 9th of this month, at 3 PM, the police suddenly closed all the doors and ordered the store to close, and successively arrested store staff, arresting and releasing them intermittently. What legal basis is there for this behavior? This kind of action is clearly destroying national products, placing our national economy and people's livelihood in a desperate situation, and treating the dignity of us Chinese people like dirt. The actual truth and the process have been reported in the newspapers for several days, and we believe you are already aware of them. We have always known that you care about the people's livelihood, and we earnestly request you to uphold justice. We are extremely eager for this."

Party Headquarters Declaration: The Fifth District Party Headquarters declared, "British imperialism has written many sad and infuriating facts in the history of its aggression against China. Even today, when our party has unified China, it has not restrained its actions. Arrogant behavior and unreasonable actions continue to emerge endlessly. Looking at the recent closure of the Chinese National Products Department Store by the Municipal Council on the pretext of reasons, the ferocious face of British imperialism is even more exposed. The tools of imperialism for invading weak nations are nothing more than three types: population oppression, political oppression, and economic oppression. Among these three, economic oppression is the most dangerous. For several years, our country has strived to fundamentally overthrow the imperialist system. The most important thing is to resist imperialist economic aggression and strive to liberate ourselves from the iron hooves of imperialist economic aggression. Under this anti-imperialist movement, promoting the national products movement is the most effective and fundamental movement. Anyone who loves the country wants to recover China's annual economic losses. Who does not agree? Unexpectedly, like a bolt from the blue, the British Municipal Council suddenly closed the department store on the pretext of reasons and arrested three staff members. Who is not shocked when the news comes? Who is not indignant? This association believes that the Municipal Council's action is definitely not for a simple notification issue. It must be intentionally destroying our country's national products movement in order to maintain its imperialist interests as its ultimate goal. We believe that this incident itself (closing a national products department store) is small, but the fact that British imperialism uses its concession privileges to oppress the Chinese and insult our national system is significant. On the one hand, we oppose the Municipal Council's closure of the department store and hope that the Municipal Council will reopen it as soon as possible and apologize. On the other hand, we must also put forward two great slogans: (1) Recover the concessions; (2) Abolish unequal treaties. Since the closing of the National Assembly, the government and the people have been striving to achieve the independence and freedom of the entire nation. We hope that the government will promptly implement the abolition of treaties and recover all concessions. This declaration is made."

National Products Association Telegram: The Shanghai National Products Factories United Association telegraphed the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Municipal Government, saying, "On the 9th of this month, the Public Concession Police dispatched police to order the National Products Department Store to close and beat and detain staff. This is not only destroying national products, but also despising national rights. If this can be tolerated, what cannot be tolerated? The association held a meeting to discuss the matter and unanimously decided to engage in serious negotiations. It was resolved that, in addition to telegraphing the central government for assistance, we also request your department to warn the Municipal Council to bear full responsibility for this provocation. This telegram is respectfully submitted for your review and implementation."

Academic Circles Expressed: More than 20 schools, including Pudong Middle School, held an emergency conference yesterday afternoon at 2 PM. Sun Yucai was publicly elected as chairman to discuss the case of the forced closure of the National Products Department Store. It was resolved that: (1) propaganda teams will set out to publicize the issue; (2) further assistance measures will be determined based on the results of negotiations with the authorities. Furthermore, the Suzhou Students Association in Shanghai dispatched Qian Daming, Li Shidu, and two other representatives to the National Products Department Store to express their condolences and offer their support.

Telegraph to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs: The Biscuit and Candy Trade Association telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, saying, "To Minister Wang of the Nanjing Ministry of Foreign Affairs: Mr. Zhang Zilian and other Shanghai merchants initiated the National Products United Department Store, intending to promote national products and resist foreign goods, which has been deeply supported by all sectors. On June 9th, the Public Concession Municipal Council, on the pretext of non-compliance with layout procedures, suddenly dispatched Chinese and foreign detectives to force the store to close, seal the doors, and arrest staff, with various destructive measures. If we do not protest strongly, national rights and people's livelihood will be completely lost. Therefore, we telegraphically request that Your Excellency promptly send a senior official to Shanghai to negotiate. We swear not to give up until we achieve victory. The telegram is urgent and we await your orders with utmost anxiety."

The Mutual Collision Case of Da Hua and Da Chang Steamers Has Not Yet Been Publicly Adjudicated 157

Because the Arbitration Conditions Have Not Yet Been Agreed Upon

Ping An Company Requests a Sincere Meeting

The Guomin News Agency says that the Da Chang steamer collided with the Da Hua steamer, causing the Da Chang steamer's engine room to leak and sink, while the bow of the Da Hua was damaged. According to the Ping An Company, the owner of the Da Hua, the Da Chang took the wrong route at the time and drove into the Da Hua's waterway. When it realized this, it hurriedly crossed the bow of the Da Hua, trying to enter the correct route, but it was too late, and the left side of the hull crashed into the bow of the Da Hua. Therefore, the accident was entirely due to the Da Chang's violation of navigation rules. The Da Hua not only had no fault beforehand but also did its best to rescue afterward. However, the Da Hua Company, the owner of the Da Chang, held a dissenting opinion on the aforementioned statement, insisting that the Ping An Company should be responsible. As for exactly why Ping An should be responsible, that is, how the Da Hua's driving was wrong, it has never provided specific details, only vaguely claiming that the Da Hua should be responsible. Since the statements of both parties differed, both agreed to submit to expert arbitration to clarify the truth. However, the arbitration requires prior agreement on the arbitration rules, specifying the number of arbitrators and the arbitration procedure, and guaranteeing that both parties have the ability to fulfill the judgment after the arbitration. In the initial consultations, the original plan was for both parties to send responsible representatives to a meeting at the Navigation Association. Ping An's attitude seemed quite sincere, but it was reported that the Da Hua Company was being manipulated by a certain insurance company regarding this case, refusing to send the Da Hua Company's manager to the meeting for sincere discussion of the contract conditions, and even wanting to invite a lawyer to attend the Navigation Association meeting to participate in the meeting. Ping An believed that this would not lead to any results, and it would be easier for the managers of the two companies to have a face-to-face and sincere discussion. The following is the letter from the Ping An Company to the Da Hua Company: "In response to your company's letter of the 8th of this month, we have learned that our company's previous letter specifically explained the identity of the representatives, for fear that one party might not be clear, so we clarified in advance to avoid misunderstandings from occurring temporarily. Moreover, the company's important staff member is Manager Ou, so we requested that the manager attend in person, precisely to express solemnity, not to impose restrictions. Now, after reading your letter, your explanation of the representatives differs from our company's opinion, and you have even changed the original agreement, in addition to wanting to appoint someone other than the company's legal representative as the representative, and also intending to add a consulting lawyer. Our company finds it difficult to agree to this new proposal. We sincerely hope that you will still follow the original agreement and the statement in our company's previous letter and sincerely discuss the conditions. If there are any further changes, our company will not be responsible for the delay." This letter is addressed to the Da Hua Company, Ping An Company, June 13, 20th year.

Tian Shulan's Ambition to Tour the Country on a Fixed Schedule 160

Departing from Shanghai to Hangzhou on July 1st

Tian Shulan, a geography professor at Minzhi Middle School, is scheduled to depart from Shanghai on a bicycle on July 1st, with the aim of touring the country in six years. According to Tian, who spoke to a reporter from the Guowen News Agency yesterday, for six or seven years, he has been working in Nanjing, teaching courses in various schools, all focusing on geography. He has always been skeptical of geography books and has observed with a comparative eye, feeling that there is a need for pragmatic research. Foreigners often come to China to investigate because of China's vast land, abundant resources, and special natural endowments. Some foreigners understand our national conditions even more precisely than our own people. This time, I (Tian said) have the ambition to tour, hoping to observe what others cannot observe, and to search for what others cannot easily search for, such as geographical formations, folk customs, scenic spots, and other data. I will complete this in six years and compile a book to contribute to the people of our country. Recently, I have been making temporary changes to the planned six-year route, depending on the conditions of each province I pass through. Tian's business card is printed with phrases such as "Traverse Divine China, Tour the Earth, The World is One Family, China is One Person." Looking at the drawing instruments, handwritten maps, military water bottles, and specially made bags placed on the wall of Tian's residence, the scene in the room is particularly unique.

Shocking News of Missing Coffin 161

Wang Ahua Murder Case

The Court Scheduled Inspection for the 15th

Yesterday Morning the Coffin Was Discovered Missing

Later Found in Reeds Far Away

Wang Fengzhou's son, Ahua, a villager from Luqitang Township in Yuepu Township, northwest of Wusong, went to Song on the 19th of last month. Through an introduction, he worked as a helper at Gao Yisheng's home in Nan Xujiawan, Zhang Huabang. Later, Ahua suddenly disappeared. Subsequently, a floating corpse was found in the Hejiaqiao River. Because it was unclaimed, the local security officer Qin Baolin put it in a coffin and placed it in a nearby public cemetery. Later, it was identified as Wang Ahua's body. Furthermore, there were many discussions outside, claiming that Ahua was beaten to death for stealing a sheep from his master Gao Yisheng's home, and the body was thrown into the river. Wang Fengzhou received this bad news and reported it to the First Branch of the Seventh District of the Public Security Bureau on the 4th of this month. The branch dispatched police to arrest the suspect Gao Yisheng and summoned the security officer Qin Baolin, Yan Chunshan, and witness Tang Arong to the case and sent it to the Local Court for investigation. Details have been recorded in this newspaper twice. The Local Court held a hearing on the case once and scheduled an inspection of the coffin on the 15th. The day before yesterday, Wang Fengzhou, the father of the deceased, received a subpoena from the court. Yesterday morning before 9 AM, he went to the public cemetery near Heqiao to inspect his son's coffin. When he arrived at the public cemetery, he was surprised to find that the heavy coffin had disappeared. He searched everywhere without a trace. Wang Fengzhou was greatly shocked. Considering the importance of the matter, he immediately took a car to Shanghai to report it to the Local Court and request an investigation. Meanwhile, he sent people everywhere to investigate the whereabouts of the coffin. It was not until around 1 PM that the coffin was found by someone in the reeds northwest of the Xujiazhai, about half a mile east of Heqiao. The most peculiar thing was that a corner of the coffin's head on the left side had been sawn off. The secret mark originally made by the corpse's family on the coffin had also been moved by a grain of rice. As for the internal condition of the coffin, it is difficult to understand for the time being. Since this strange incident occurred, people from far and near have been flocking to watch, and all are greatly astonished.

Ye Chen Reconciliation Terms 163

Ye Pays 3,000 Yuan in One Lump Sum

The Man and Woman Will Have No Further Relationship From Now On

Ye Zhongfang and Chen Xiuzhen have been in litigation for several months, which has not been resolved. This newspaper has reported on it many times. Since Chen returned to her mother's house, Ye has still been unable to forget Chen, even wanting to mend the broken mirror. Later, Ye's relatives and friends and lawyer Dong Yu repeatedly persuaded Zhongfang, and he finally agreed to painfully sever the emotional ties and decided to end the husband-concubine relationship with Xiuzhen. On the one hand, the lawyer applied to the court for an extension of the trial period, and on the other hand, he proceeded with reconciliation. It has been three weeks, but the conditions have delayed the reconciliation. It is now reported that Dong Yu, the lawyer, invited Ye Zhongfang and Chen Xiuzhen's lawyer Yao Zhaodi, etc., to continue discussing the reconciliation terms at Dong's law firm the night before yesterday. At that time, both parties were able to understand each other and were willing to settle peacefully. The reconciliation contract they signed was roughly as follows: (1) From the date of signing this contract, Chen Xiuzhen and Ye Zhongfang will terminate all relations arising from cohabitation. In the future, both parties will be free to marry and live their own lives. (2) After Chen Xiuzhen leaves Ye Zhongfang, she is free to choose her profession, and Ye Zhongfang will not interfere. If Chen Xiuzhen becomes a dancer again, she must not ask him to accompany her, so as not to cause misunderstandings. (3) Ye Zhongfang and Ye Pengshi should jointly and severally pay Chen Xiuzhen and Chen Yanshi 3,000 yuan in cash within three days, and return Chen Xiuzhen's clothes and ornaments left in Ye's home, including a diamond-studded watch and two diamond rings, to Chen Xiuzhen. The recipient will issue a separate receipt as proof. (4) Once Ye Zhongfang and Ye Pengshi fulfill the above conditions and deliver the money, clothes, and ornaments, all parties will withdraw the cases they have already filed and will not cause any further disputes. After both parties agreed, they wrote five identical copies of the reconciliation contract for Ye Zhongfang, Chen Xiuzhen, Ye Pengshi, Chen Yanshi, Ye Lushi, and the certifying lawyers Jiang Yiping, Dong Yu, and Yao Zhaodi, and all the above-mentioned names signed and sealed the documents. The two lawyers, Dong Yu and Yao Zhaodi, yesterday filed separate petitions with the Special District Court and the French Court, requesting the withdrawal of the cases.

Lost Girl Regrets 164

Sad Events Bring Tears

Jumped into Huangpu River, Fortunately Rescued

At 0:40 AM yesterday morning, at the Public Concession Hospital pier in Suzhou Creek, a young woman wearing a cheongsam and with short hair, suddenly jumped into the river to commit suicide when no one was on the shore. Fortunately, she was spotted by Hua, a patrolman from the Seventh Station of the Maritime Customs Police Station, who immediately stepped forward and rescued her, allowing her to be reborn. She was taken to the police station by the patrolman. According to her confession, her surname is Chen, her name is Xuanying, also known as Huizhen, she is 17 years old, from Suzhou, and lives on the third floor of the Kotada Yoko shoe store at No. 200 Seymour Road, Jing'an Temple Road. Her father's name is Youyue, and she has a stepmother, two older sisters, one older brother, one sister-in-law, and one younger brother. Four months before today, the owner of the shoe store, Guan, talked to me from time to time and accompanied me to the cinema. According to him, he was not married and revealed his admiration for me, further proposing to me. However, I did not express my consent at the time,

Whether or not to agree. Since then, Guan has become even more intimate with me. I was confused for a while, thinking that free love was not a shameful thing, so a month ago, we went to the Shenzhou Hotel on Fourth Horse Road together for one night. Afterwards, we went to the Gaosheng Hotel on Fifth Horse Road for two nights. A moment of error, lost my virginity forever. Eventually, the matter was discovered by my family because it was not kept secret. My father became even more furious and recently drove me out of the house, saying that I was shameless and should not come home again, shaming the Chen family, etc. Unable to do otherwise, I planned to find a place to live temporarily, so I made an appointment with Guan to discuss finding a house to live together. Unexpectedly, Guan was iron-hearted and cold, abandoned me, making me a helpless orphan who had not yet entered the world. I had nowhere to turn. I wanted to go home and beg my parents to forgive my momentary foolishness and take me in, but I did not have the courage to do so. In the end, I decided to die to get rid of my troubles, etc. According to the police chief, seeing that she was very pitiful, he ordered Detective Wu Rongsheng to escort her to the Local Court at 2 PM yesterday to seek relief.

Zhou Huanzhang and Wife in Protracted Litigation 172

Verdict Scheduled for the 19th of This Month

Zhou Huanzhang, residing at No. 102, Siwen Li, Dagu Road, has been in the bamboo business. At the age of eight, he was betrothed to Xu, who was only seven years old at the time. They married at the age of nineteen and are now forty-three years old. They have a son named Dongquan, who is now twenty-four years old and studying at Great China University, and a second son, Dongxing, who is also twenty-two years old and studying at the Faculty of Law. They have an elderly mother at home, and in theory, the family should be harmonious and happy. However, the couple is now separated, the mother and sons rarely see each other, and the grandparents and grandchildren are often apart. Recently, his wife, Zhou Xushi, filed a complaint with the Special District Court, accusing him of neglecting support and demanding cohabitation. Her complaint stated that she was betrothed to the Zhou family at a young age and married at eighteen. However, the family was poor at the time, and her late uncle had a Zhou Yida bamboo shop. The plaintiff and defendant worked together to manage the shop, and after more than ten years of hard work, the situation improved, and they successively purchased more than thirty mu of land in Shanghai. Unfortunately, her late uncle passed away in 1920, and the defendant secretly cohabited with a certain woman. Since December 30, 1923, he has not stepped foot in the house for nine years. Although the eldest son was raised by an aunt, the second son was only twelve years old and the third daughter, A'gen, was only nine years old, and their upbringing and education required expenses. The daughter, seeing her husband's heartlessness, could only sigh and hope for his repentance. However, the defendant monopolized the family property, and the children's food and clothing depended on her ten fingers and the annual rent of 1,200 taels from the land on the Suzhou Riverbank on Maigen Road. Recently, her strength has declined, and the land has been sold by her husband for 50,000 to 60,000 taels. The tenant demanded the return of the rent fee of 1,000 taels, claiming that the lease term had not expired. He refused to pay for the children's schooling and living expenses, hence the lawsuit. In the first instance, the defendant failed to appear twice after being summoned, and the court ruled that the allegations were well-founded based on the evidence. The 1,000 taels of land rent was declared to be alimony due and was subject to provisional execution. The defendant Zhou Huanzhang, dissatisfied with the judgment, hired lawyer Yu Hualong to file an appeal. Yesterday was the joint hearing, and all parties were present. The grounds for the appeal stated that the appellant had land on the Suzhou Riverbank, which was privately leased by Zhou and received an annual rent of 1,200 taels, which she pocketed. Recently, the land was bought by the Public Works Bureau for road construction, and 1,000 taels had already been collected from the tenant in advance, which should be returned by Zhou. As for the alimony portion, when they separated in 1921, Zhou obtained the Zhou Yida North Shop, with inventory worth 7,000 to 8,000 yuan, plus the income from leasing the base over the years, which was considerable and sufficient for Zhou and her children's future living expenses. Moreover, there were eight rooms on Maigen Road, which could collect more than 70 yuan in rent per month, so it could not be said that he neglected support. Furthermore, after his father's death, Zhou wanted to drive out the appellant's mother, causing constant disturbances, which was the subject of a lawsuit in the former Mixed Court, leading to their separation. At that time, half of the family property, the Zhou Yida Bamboo Shop, was given to her to occupy exclusively for her livelihood, which could be said to be benevolent and righteous. As for the request for cohabitation, he also agreed. When his mother was summoned, she testified that after her husband's death, the son and daughter-in-law had disagreements and often quarreled, so her husband left behind the Zhou Yida North and South Bamboo Shops, and the son and daughter-in-law each lived in one shop. When the daughter-in-law returned, she would always quarrel and leave, and she bore the cost of the eldest grandson's tuition, etc. Then, his sons, Dongquan and Dongxing, were summoned and ordered to mediate, and they testified that the younger generation had no room to intervene in this matter and requested the court to handle it impartially. After further debate by both lawyers, the prosecutor's opinion was that the 1,000 taels of rent should be returned by the appellant, Zhou Huanzhang should give Zhou a monthly living allowance of 30 to 40 yuan, and the father should be responsible for the tuition of the two sons. The court announced that the verdict would be delivered on the 19th of this month.

Screening of Pornographic Films 174

Mastermind Arrested After Being Discovered by Police

In Shanghai, all kinds of strange things emerge endlessly. The concession authorities conduct strict investigations but cannot completely eliminate them. Recently, Chinese and Western detectives from the Laozha Gate Police Station, based on secret reports from informants, discovered that the China Hotel behind the Xinxin Company on Guizhou Road often had unscrupulous individuals screening obscene pornographic films to attract tourists. The police investigated several times but did not obtain any real evidence. Until yesterday, Laozha Gate detective You Fugen discovered that several hooligans in Room 220 of the China Hotel had opened a room to screen this kind of obscene film. The police believed that if this kind of obscene drama was not quickly banned, it would be detrimental to public morals and security, and immediately ordered Chinese and Western detectives to arrest them. When they arrived, the perpetrators were crowded in a room, enjoying themselves, and their minds were muddled. The detectives arrested the masterminds, Kong Zhangfu and Lu Chunsheng, as well as three tea waiters and the projectionist, and seized a reel of film and a projector, and took them to the police station. The next morning, they were sent to the Special District Court for interrogation. Kong and Lu confessed that they were in the foreign goods business and lived at No. 766 Beijing Road. The judge said that since they were legitimate businessmen, they should not commit such illegal acts that harm society and ordered each of them to post 1,000 yuan in cash as bail, and sent the other two to the police station for detention, and scheduled a retrial for Thursday.

Two People Commit Suicide by Poison 175

㈠ On the 11th, a man from Suzhou checked into the Laodexing Inn at No. 155, McGao Baolu Road in the French Concession, claiming to be Yuan Mingzhi, 25 years old, and in the foreign goods business. He opened Room 1 and paid five dimes for the room, then closed the door and went to sleep. Yuan, feeling that the environment was bad, became tired of the world and committed suicide by smoking raw opium. At about 1 p.m. on the 11th, the tea waiter went to knock on the door, but there was no response after a long time. Knowing that something was wrong, he managed to pry open the door and saw Yuan's face was pale and his breath was weak. On the table in front of the bed, there was still a box of raw opium and six pieces of banana candy. He immediately reported to the accounting office, which reported to the Songshan Road Police Station. He was sent to Renji Hospital for treatment, but he died at 12:30 p.m. yesterday and was sent to the mortuary to await burial. ㈡ Li Baoming, 24 years old, from Pudong, was in the foreign goods business. At 9:30 p.m. the day before yesterday, he pre-purchased opium and opened Room 6 at the Fuxing Inn at No. 70, Avenue Joffre in the French Concession, paying five dimes for the room, then closed the door and went to bed. At 10 a.m. yesterday, the tea waiter heard a miserable groan from the room and knew that something was wrong. He broke down the door and entered, and saw Li lying stiffly in bed, his face pale and unable to speak. Knowing that he had taken poison, he reported to the accounting office, which reported to the Songshan Road Police Station. He was sent to Renji Hospital for treatment, but he died at about 1 p.m. and was sent to the forensic examination office to await examination.

The Businesses on Limalu and Dadatou Submit a Document to the Municipal Government 177

Requesting a Postponement of House Demolition

The businesses on Limalu and Dadatou in Nanshi have been notified by the Land and Public Works Bureau to demolish their houses by a certain deadline. They believe that the deadline is too short and that they will not be able to relocate in time, and there is nowhere to move to. They have submitted separate documents to the Municipal Government and the Land and Public Works Bureau, stating: "We are submitting this document to request that you take into consideration the difficulties of the businesses and the livelihoods of the workers, and postpone the demolition of the houses so that we can make amends. We, the businesses located on Limalu and Dadatou, have been operating for many years. We have read the announcements issued jointly by your bureau and the Land (Public Works) Bureau, and we have also received notices stating that the project to reorganize the road line on the northern section of Limalu and the eastern section of Dadatou is very important and should be widened as soon as possible so that it can be completed. It is now stipulated that all houses on this road must be demolished by the end of June of this year so that construction can begin. We understand that the houses we rent are all to be demolished. We admire your government (bureau)'s efforts to build and revitalize the city. However, we must also ask you to consider the difficulties of the businesses and the importance of the livelihoods of the workers. According to Shanghai custom, landlords must notify businesses and tenants at least three months or half a year in advance if they want them to move so that they can prepare. However, the date we received the notice from the landlord is only one month before the stipulated deadline. We are very alarmed by this urgency. Shanghai is a densely populated city, and it is difficult to find hundreds of empty houses at the same time. Even if we find a few houses, it will be impossible to complete the procedures for negotiating prices, moving goods, and clearing accounts in time. Moreover, the location of the market may not be suitable for business. If hundreds of businesses are demolished, they will inevitably close down, and the thousands of workers they employ will lose their jobs. The construction project is huge and will not be completed in a short time. For a long time, the families of those who rely on their daily income will have nowhere to turn. The livelihoods of thousands of people are at stake and cannot be ignored. Each business has goods in storage, which is where their capital lies, and they cannot be abandoned. Even if there is a place to store them, fresh goods will spoil if stored for a long time, and goods that can be stored for a long time rely on brisk sales to turn over their costs. Otherwise, they will have no source of income and disputes will inevitably arise. Furthermore, the accounts that each business has extended this year are not small. Once the stores are closed, how will they be collected? All of these matters concern the capital of the businesses and the financial stability of the market. We, the businesses, are compelled to discuss this matter together and want to find a place to move so that the thousands of workers will not be completely displaced, the extended accounts can be recovered, and the losses will not be too great. We sincerely request that you consider the difficulties of the businesses and allow us to postpone the demolition until the end of February of next year (i.e., after the end of the current year's accounting) and then begin the demolition and construction in stages, so that both municipal administration and business conditions can be taken into account. We are eagerly awaiting your orders." This document is respectfully submitted by Zhang, the Mayor of Shanghai Municipality, Zhu, the Director of the Land Bureau, and Shen, the Director of the Public Works Bureau, as well as Fengtai, Yuanlai, Tonghe, Zhisheng, Yufeng, Yuanfeng, Huichang, Yuanyucheng, Heta, Hongchangyu, Changyu, Shunji, Fahe, Hengji, Hengyuan, Wancheng, Shentai, Chunmaohe, Wanxing, Yongda, etc.

New Weights and Measures System Implemented in This City 179

Inspections Began the Day Before Yesterday

Concession Authorities Assisting in Implementation

There are many types of weights and measures in China. Not only are there differences between different regions and industries, but even within the same region and industry, there is no consistency. This has caused deep-seated problems that affect the livelihood of the people and are of great consequence. Previously, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce convened a meeting of provinces and cities to discuss the implementation of a new system of weights and measures, promulgated regulations, and ordered all provinces and cities to comply accordingly. This city is promoting the aforementioned new system, and the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has urged the Weights and Measures Verification Office to actively proceed according to a uniform procedure. Currently, the uniformity of various vegetable markets in the city has begun. It is reported that the Verification Office, together with the public security organs, sends police to inspect each one every day. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency, believing that this matter concerns municipal construction and wanting to understand the implementation situation, visited the Verification Office on Xieqiao Manufacturing Bureau Road to observe its contents. There were countless large and small weighing instruments stored inside. The staff of the office were very busy, working an extra hour each morning and evening (7 a.m. to 6 p.m.). The following is an excerpt from an interview with the director of the office, Zhou: (Reporter asks) What is the new system? (Answer) There are two systems in the new system: one is the standard system, which adopts the international metric system, and the other is the municipal system, which is suitable for civilian habits. (Question) What is the difference between the municipal system and the standard system? (Answer) The standard system is the French system, which is very convenient for decimal calculation. However, it is somewhat different from civilian habits, so a municipal system that is most convenient for conversion with the standard system has been formulated. The municipal system is also known as the one-two-three system, that is, one standard liter is equal to one municipal liter, one standard jin is equal to two municipal jin, and one standard chi is equal to three municipal chi, hence the name one-two-three system. In fact, the standard system and the municipal system are one and two and three and one. Moreover, the relationship between the two is very easy to remember. (Question) How much does the municipal system differ from the old weights and measures? (Answer) There are too many types of old systems, with different sizes and weights. Therefore, when people usually say a few jin, they must specify what kind of scale and how many jin, otherwise it is impossible to know its absolute weight or quantity. Therefore, I can only answer what kind of old weights and measures it is equivalent to and how much, otherwise it is impossible to be clear. Generally speaking, one municipal chi is equal to 9.37 inches of a tailor's ruler, one municipal hu is equal to 8.452 dou of a sea hu, one municipal jin is equal to 12.988 qian of a Sima scale, 15.15 qian of a guild scale, and 13.64 fen of a balance scale. (Question) Has the vegetable market been changed to the new system? (Answer) The original plan was to start using new instruments in the vegetable market on June 1. The day before yesterday, inspectors were sent to inspect the Tangjiawan and Hongqiao vegetable markets together with the police from the Public Security Bureau. The results were very good. In the past, buyers often used heavy scales, which often led to disputes between buyers and sellers. Now there is a uniform method, and all the vendors in the vegetable market welcome it. (Question) There are very few factories and shops in this city that manufacture weights and measures. If new instruments are used one day, will there be a shortage of supply? (Answer) You are right. This is an unavoidable thing in the transitional era. However, the Social Affairs Bureau and our office have long foreseen this and have been urging the manufacturing factories and shops to prepare early this year. However, the merchants were waiting and watching, so there was not much inventory. Two months ago, the Municipal Government allocated funds to recruit merchants to jointly establish a Weights and Measures New Instrument Manufacturing Factory Co., Ltd. to engage in manufacturing and sales. Only then did the shops dare to boldly manufacture new instruments in large quantities. Currently, the company has accumulated more than 20,000 large and small lever scales, which are currently sufficient to meet the needs of various vegetable markets. One side is rushing to build, and our office is afraid that the shops will take the opportunity to raise prices, so we have specifically stipulated uniform prices and strictly prohibited hoarding. (Question) Are these new instruments sold by various factories outside? (Answer) Yes, but the production capacity of each shop owner is weak and there is not much inventory. They are not as well-funded and large-scale as the company established by the Municipal Government. If you want to order goods, you can contact them directly. The company's office is located in our office, which is more convenient. (Question) Is the price of the company the same as the price of each factory? (Answer) Completely the same. (Question) The date for the city's uniformity is approaching. Will it be handled uniformly in the Special Zone within the time limit in the future? (Answer) Regarding the implementation of the new system in the Special Zone, we have discussed with the authorities of the Public Concession and the French Concession, the Chinese Taxpayers' Association, and the Special District Court several times. The implementation method is generally no problem. After all, there are precedents in various countries for uniform weights and measures. Our office will carry out the national laws and regulations and will of course proceed consistently. Now the concession authorities have expressed their support for the implementation.

Eighty-First Meeting

The Shanghai Lawyers Association convened its 81st joint meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees at 8 p.m. last night. The resolutions proposed by our association were passed, except for the Notary Public Law, which was not sympathized with due to conflicts with the legislative intent of the Legislative Yuan and the notary public laws of the United States and Britain. In addition, it was resolved to organize the International Lawyers Association and elect our association as the chief of the preparatory committee. The intention was to achieve the goal of abolishing consular jurisdiction in the International Association. Regarding the expenses, it cost 70,000 to 80,000 yuan to hold meetings in the Philippines and Japan in the past, while it is proposed to prepare 200,000 yuan in our country. This amount is not small, and it is proposed that the government bear the preparatory expenses, first agreeing to 5,000 yuan. This amount will be used to publish various legal books in our country for the purpose of promoting the Chinese legal system, which will be borne by the Shanghai, Hangzhou, Beiping, and Jiangning associations and paid in four installments. The location will be in Shanghai, and the Beiping Lawyers Association has many Japanese books, which were obtained from the International Lawyers Association meeting, and these books can be transferred to our association. Regarding this matter, the liaison with the government will be handled by Committee Member Chen Zemin, and the minutes of the first preparatory meeting of the International Lawyers Association were submitted for discussion. Then, Committee Member Chen Zemin reported on the process of contacting Foreign Minister Wang Rutang in Beijing, who was willing to help, and supplemented that our country had previously prepared to open the International Lawyers Association and had initially obtained the consent of more than 20 countries around the world, but it was not implemented due to funding problems. Moreover, the criminal law issue has changed slightly, and the world's criminal law is more inclined to the criminal law of Siam. However, this criminal law is based on our country's ancient criminal law as a blueprint, while our country adopts the Western five major legal systems of the Chinese legal system, which has fallen into obscurity. Therefore, there is an opportunity to launch this conference and promote the Chinese legal system as much as possible. After Tan Yigong, Li Shirui, Cai Nipei, Zhang Feixiong, and others expressed their opinions, it was resolved that this case is an important relationship. The minutes of the first preparatory meeting of the International Lawyers Association were passed and submitted to the extraordinary general meeting on the 14th of this month for decision. ㈡ The Jiangsu Higher Court instructed to interpret legal ambiguities. If it is a matter of personal qualifications, it is not appropriate to forward the request for interpretation. It was resolved that cases of interpretation of legal ambiguities will not be listed in the name of individuals in the future to avoid non-compliance with the conditions. ㈢ The Shanghai District Court Procuratorate issued an order to investigate whether lawyer Gu Yongquan's practice outside the district violated the Lawyers' Regulations. It was resolved to send a letter to member Gu to reply. ㈣ The Anhui Shanghai Fellow Association reported that an American sailor stabbed a fellow villager and requested that the association negotiate. It was resolved to introduce member Wu Jingxiong to provide voluntary assistance and send a letter to the association for verification. ㈤ The China National Products Commercial Market reported that British imperialists were oppressing and blockading the commercial market on the pretext and requested assistance. It was resolved to hand it over to the Standing Committee for handling and send a letter to the commercial market for verification. ㈥ Lawyers Shen Chenju, Yang Liufeng, Wen Zhenlin, Mao Yun, Sha Yunxiang, Xia Xunqi, and Hu Yuanteng applied for membership. It was resolved to pass. ㈦ Member Ni Gang reported that the fifth district and third branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau insulted a lawyer and requested that the Municipal Public Security Bureau investigate. It was resolved to hand it over to the Standing Committee for handling. The meeting adjourned late at night after the discussions.

Navigation Administration Actively Preparing 181

The Bureau Address Has Now Been Found

Registration and Inspection Matters

Since the Ministry of Communications appointed Xi Dingmo as the director of the Shanghai Navigation Administration, preparations have been underway and are exceptionally busy. The current status of preparations and the outline of the internal organization are recorded below:

Recent Preparations According to Xi's interview with a reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency yesterday, after I was ordered, I immediately started planning and proceeding. Since this is the first time that our country has officially established a Navigation Administration, the first difficulty I felt was the issue of talent. In our country, there are very few excellent navigation administration talents, and even those with slightly more experience are not many. After I searched in many ways, I reluctantly found three or four people. The office location has now been found on the second floor of the new building at No. 6 Sichuan Road, Aiduya Road. The building is still under construction and is expected to be completed around the 20th of this month. Once it is completed, I plan to start arranging it. As for the transfer of the Shipping Administration Bureau of the Customs Service, the Ministry of Communications has consulted the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Finance has ordered the Customs to handle the handover. Once the Navigation Administration is officially established, it can be taken over.

Organizational Outline Regarding the internal organization, in addition to the director, there are two section chiefs and eight technicians. According to the provisions of the Maritime Law, they will handle maritime affairs, and the most important of these are about four types: ㈠ Registration, regardless of whether it is a Chinese or foreign ship, its tonnage, draft, and pilots and seafarers must be registered with the Navigation Administration for assessment. ㈡ Inspection, the equipment of the ship, the weight of the cargo, the qualifications of the driver, etc., must be inspected by personnel when entering and leaving, and a permit must be issued before allowing travel. ㈢ Nationality Passport, ships of all countries have nationality passports, but our country only has ministerial passports. The nationality passport is still lacking. In the future, if our country's shipping industry wants to develop abroad, this procedure is indispensable. Therefore, after the Navigation Administration is established, it must handle this work. ㈣ Measurement, in the future, the length and width of ships must be measured to check the amount of its capacity. In addition, the drawings of newly built ships must be submitted to the bureau for approval in advance, etc., which are more important.
