Yesterday's News of the Guanghua Factory Labor Strike 185

All the workers of the Guanghua Dyeing and Weaving Factory on Luban Road in this city, due to resisting the oppression of the factory manager Gu Yongquan, incited public outrage and caused a dispute. More than one hundred labor unions in the city have jointly decided on various disposal measures, which are selected as follows: ㈠ Sending representatives to the party and government to petition. Yesterday morning, representatives Zhao Shusheng, Wang Wenhua, Lu Muqin, Gu Ruofeng, and others were specially sent to meet with Zhang Tinghao, section chief of the Social Affairs Bureau, and the Civil Training Association of the City Party Department, to express their extreme dissatisfaction with Gu Yongquan's oppressive behavior. They intend to stop him from working in Shanghai to avoid causing similar disputes. ㈡ Labor unions have donated funds to help. The Shanghai Postal Workers Union donated thirty yuan, the Shanghai Postal Workers Union donated ten yuan, the Water and Electricity Workers Union donated ten yuan, and other labor unions have also donated a considerable amount. ㈢ Joint Declaration (The Shanghai Labor Unions' Declaration on the Guanghua Dyeing and Weaving Factory Labor Strike is as follows: We, the more than 300 workers of the Guanghua Dyeing and Weaving Factory, unable to endure the trampling and oppression of the factory manager Gu Yongquan, stomp our feet and beat our chests, crying in pain and despair, almost falling into a situation where we cannot live or die. We and others have witnessed this with heartache. In order to save the dying workers and maintain the healthy development of the labor movement, we have to speak out righteously and report to all sectors of society. It is found that Gu Yongquan was originally a worker in a mercerized factory and one of the responsible persons of the former Mercerized Factory Union. (Omission) In March of this year, he resigned from his position in the labor union and jumped to become the factory manager. Within just over two months of taking office, he arbitrarily set unreasonable factory rules and treated workers harshly. More than 140 workers were given demerits for minor or even no reason, and more than 70 workers were fired. Our workers crawled under Gu Yongquan's licentious power, weeping silently and daring not to speak. Unfortunately, worker Zhu Linhou, on the day of this month, during working hours when the machine was in operation, his clothes were suddenly splashed with medicated soapy water. In order to prevent his clothes and skin from being burned, the worker took off his clothes and washed them himself. Unexpectedly, Gu Yongquan became angry and accused him of violating factory rules and neglecting work, and immediately fired Zhu Linhou. After repeated negotiations by the labor union, he was allowed to return to work, but he had to write a letter of repentance. However, on the day of this month, when Zhu Linhou went to work, Gu Yongquan again used the letter of repentance as an excuse, claiming that the wording did not match, and unreasonably forced Zhu Linhou to leave the factory, and even added unbearable insults. All the workers in the factory were unanimously indignant and expressed their resistance. Gu Yongquan concealed the military and political authorities and falsely accused them of riots and strikes, and successively reported to the Public Security Bureau and the Garrison Command. On the day of this month, seventeen innocent workers, including Jiang A'er, were arrested by the Public Security Bureau. Afterwards, the party and government sent personnel to investigate. We and others could not bear to sit idly by, so we urgently listed the crimes, urged the party and government organs to provide assistance, release the workers, and expel Gu Yongquan from the party, remove him from his post, and send him to the court to be dealt with according to the law for the crime of false accusation and concealment, so as to serve as a warning to those who are unrepentant. The Shanghai Postal Workers Union, the Publishing Industry Union, and more than one hundred other labor unions, 206, 13, the Shanghai Dyeing Industry Workers Union, and the Mercerized Factory held an emergency representative meeting yesterday, publicly electing Liu Jintai as chairman, and performing the rituals. (A) Reporting items: ㈠ The process of Guanghua Factory manager Gu Yongquan deliberately causing a labor strike; ㈡ The process of Yan A'er and other seventeen people from Guanghua Factory being arrested; ㈢ Gu Yongquan's coercion of workers to sign contracts; (B) Discussion and decision items: ㈠ The case of assisting the arrested comrades of the Guanghua Factory, decided to have all members of each factory petition to the higher authorities; ㈡ The case of expelling Gu Yongquan from the Guanghua Factory to ensure work stability, decided to submit a request to the higher authorities for investigation; ㈢ The case of how to handle the Guanghua Factory's forcible contract and oppression of workers, decided to unanimously deny and broadly request the higher authorities to immediately revoke it.

The Tariff Commission Requests Approval to Reduce Export Tariffs 186

The Various Industries Tariff Research Committee submitted a report to the National Government yesterday, requesting approval to reduce export tariffs on tung oil and other industries. The original report stated: "The report is submitted to request approval to reduce export tariffs on tung oil, tobacco leaves, firecrackers, and other industries, in order to maintain commerce and benefit the people. Since the promulgation of the new export tariffs, merchants and people of various industries have repeatedly telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, claiming that the burden has increased. However, the Ministry's reply was that the case had been reviewed and approved by the Legislative Yuan, and the National Government had issued a clear order for implementation, so the Ministry could not revise it, resulting in the tariff rate not being reduced, which has indeed affected the progress of export trade. This special summary report is hereby submitted to your government, requesting that it be forwarded for approval and reduction, and hoping that you will take note of it. ㈠ The export tariff rate for the tung oil industry has been increased by a huge amount of 2.56 times. At a time when the United States is vigorously planting tung trees and exports are being squeezed by Japan, the tax-paying price should be re-estimated and lightly revised to avoid repeating the mistakes of the silk and tea industries. ㈡ The export tariff rate for tobacco leaves is 7.5%, and each dan must pay one tael and seven qian, which is more than eleven times the old tax of one qian and five fen per dan. Moreover, the governments of various countries have repeatedly increased the import tax on Chinese tobacco leaves, and the export trade of domestic tobacco leaves has been severely hit. If a high export tax is levied domestically, it will be difficult to survive. It is requested that it be forwarded for light revision to maintain it. ㈢ The export tax on firecrackers is one tael and two qian per dan, which is more than seven qian more than the original tariff rate. Firecrackers are entirely handmade products, and millions of workers and merchants in the country rely on them for their livelihoods. The annual sales abroad are very large. Taking Annam as an example, according to French statistics in 1925, it was worth six million francs. Considering the government's main purpose of encouraging the development of handicrafts and foreign trade, it seems that it should be specially reduced, and the raw materials for the product are paper, nitrate, and sulfur, which have all been taxed, so the tariff rate should be further reduced to avoid affecting costs. It is reasonable to submit a written summary report to your government, hoping that you will review and approve it, and allow it to be forwarded for separate light revisions, in order to maintain commerce and benefit the people, which is very fair."

The Federation of Machine Industries Requests Exemption from Business Tax for the Paint Industry 187

The Shanghai Federation of Machine Industries submitted a document to the Ministry of Finance, saying: "The report is submitted to truthfully forward the request for exemption from business tax. It is reported that the members Kailin, Yonggu, Yonghua, Zhenhua, and other four paint companies stated in their letters that they had previously read in the newspaper that the business tax rate for the Shanghai Municipality's draft manufacturing industry tax rate item was 10% of the capital amount. According to our companies' manufacture of paint, it has long been approved to be treated as machine-made foreign-style goods, and it is generally exempt from repeated taxation when transported and sold domestically, and completely exempt from taxation when exported abroad. It should be based on the original case, and we earnestly request your association to forward the request to the Ministry of Finance for exemption from business tax, which is really a matter of public interest. It is based on this, and it is found that the government is undertaking business tax in order to offset the tax revenue of likin. However, machine-made foreign-style goods approved in the original case can be exempted from likin, and should be exempt from business tax. It is found that the implementation of business tax in Shanghai Municipality is imminent, and the tax rate for the paint manufacturing industry is 10% of the capital amount, which does not seem to be in line with the government's intention to promote domestic goods and encourage industry. It is really necessary to submit a request for exemption, so this special report is submitted truthfully, hoping that your ministry will review and approve it, and allow the business tax for the paint manufacturing industry to be exempted from collection, in order to alleviate the difficulties of merchants and promote industry, which is very convenient. Respectfully presented to the Ministry of Finance of the Executive Yuan of the National Government) The Ministry of Finance's No. 12947 decree replied, "The report is noted. The city's business tax collection regulations should be consulted and verified by the Ministry, and after a decision is made, it will be forwarded for compliance." This approval (a separate document submitted to the municipal government is omitted)

Guo Yuan's Suicide by Hanging 191

Guo Dianxiang, a native of Funing, who lived at No. 98 Beijing Jiang Road in Zha, has been in the second-hand goods business. He and his wife, Yuan, have been married for many years, and their relationship is still good. Guo has been plagued by illness in recent years, has been unemployed for several years, and is in extremely difficult financial straits. They are often worried about running out of food. Yuan is not accustomed to the cold and hardship. At first, she sighed that her life was thin and relied on the income from her ten fingers to maintain her livelihood. Then, feeling angry that her husband's chronic illness was not improving, she often said that it would be better to die than to live in suffering. Her husband had heard it so often that he didn't take it seriously. Unexpectedly, the night before last, they quarreled over a trivial matter. She went straight to the bedroom, found a hemp rope, tied it to the roof beam, and hanged herself. When Guo went inside, he saw that the light was off and was very surprised. Feeling around in the dark, he was shocked to find his wife's feet dangling in the air. He quickly lit a fire and saw that she was already dead. He held her body and wailed loudly. He was reported to the Fourth District General Office by his co-residents. Yesterday afternoon, an appointed prosecutor came to inspect the body and ordered it to be collected and buried first, while Guo was detained for questioning.

Free Talk

World Anecdotes 207

— Hai Ke

When Europeans and Americans travel to the tropics, they often first place the ship's clocks on an electric stove to bake them. When exploring the Arctic, they first freeze the clocks in a refrigerator to test whether the clock mechanism can withstand extreme heat and cold.

Ms. H. Winter, a blind British woman, is blind in sight but not in mind. She once won a public history exam and was sent to Oxford University for further study. She has now graduated. The books she uses daily are all in raised characters, donated by people enthusiastic about education.

An American insurance company's statistics on policyholder injuries show that injuries occurring on sports fields are five times more frequent than accidents on streetcars, trains, and ships.

The Royal Academy of Arts in England selected art works for 1931. The number of works with the qualification to be reviewed included 4,303 oil paintings, 3,443 watercolors, 1,209 sketches, and 643 sculptures. The final number of selected works in all four categories totaled only 1,436.

Several major roads in Germany will be equipped with nine different colored lights on the light poles on both sides of the road to guide car drivers. Wherever they plan to go, they simply follow the lights of that color.

Remembering the Martyrs Liang Tingdong and Tingyue, Brothers Who Died for Their Cause 208

— Fang Chuqiu

The revolutionary wind, our Anhui sang it the earliest. It should be the Liang martyrs Tingdong brothers on the Huai River. The martyr's name is Shiqing. He lived in Shouxian, Anhui. He was benevolent and resolute. He liked to make friends and was chivalrous. In the late Qing Guangxu years, seeing that the country was declining day by day, he traveled around to make friends widely. Wherever he went, he always used the meaning of reform to guide people as the opportunity arose. He braved dangers and difficulties for more than ten years. When he arrived in Hebei, he said with emotion: Yan and Zhao have been known since ancient times for having many generous and tragic scholars. Although their atmosphere is closed, it can be opened with great righteousness. So he lived in Peiping. At that time, he was very close with officers and soldiers of the Yi Army. Many old comrades went to rely on him. When Qing Xuantong succeeded to the throne, Zai Feng was regent. Empress Dowager Longyu wanted to pursue the matter of the Wuxu coup and put Yuan Shikai on trial. The military and civilians were in a panic. The martyr secretly conspired with Yi Army comrades to take the opportunity to launch an uprising. It was leaked by those who were fond of profit. The government demanded it urgently. So he took the indirect route to Jilin, hid in Changchun, and changed his name to Liang Qingyu. Comrades continued to arrive. Because of insufficient funds, he sold articles for a living. His younger brother Tingyue, whose name was Zhuoqing, was naturally filial and friendly, excelled in languages, and was proficient in epigraphy, arithmetic, and music. Feeling that his brother's aspirations were not fulfilled, he used education to seek progress and advocated private school reform. He took on the role of professor without accepting a salary, and took pleasure in people's pleasure and worried about people's worries. After a long time, many friends and followers. Those who were jealous framed him. The county official suspected him. Although the disaster was hidden, his spirit was not diminished. Soon, he obeyed his mother's order to go to Changchun to meet his brother Tingdong. When he arrived, his third brother Tinghuai was already there. Tinghuai, also known as Bing, whose name was Yinqing, was a comrade of Tingdong from a young age. Earlier, the Xiong martyr Chengji launched an uprising in Anhui. After the defeat, he went to Japan and then to Jilin. Tinghuai conspired from Peiping and advocated righteousness in the three eastern provinces. Soon Xiong was sold by Zang Guansan and arrested. Tinghuai's Peiping residence was searched. Jilin Governor Chen Zhaochang secretly telegraphed the Qing court. The purchase and arrest were very urgent, but Tinghuai escaped upon hearing the news and went to Changchun. In the autumn of Xinhai, the Wuchang uprising broke out. The whole country responded. Tingdong and his brothers discussed with their comrades: The inland is gradually being restored. The three eastern provinces are important border areas. Zhao Erxun and others hold troops to consolidate themselves and plan to resist. If we do not quickly break it, they will surely support the small court and call on Manchuria and Mongolia, and use Japanese and Russian diplomacy to contain it. Although the Southern Army is strong, there will be worries that the whip is beyond its reach. It is appropriate to gather the people's army and raise the banner of righteousness to support the Central Plains. So comrades Liu Qianyi, Shang Zhen, etc. in Fengtian publicly elected Lan Tianwei as the Grand Governor of Guanwai, and the martyr Kun promoted the affairs of Jilin and Heilongjiang. The agency was set up in Harbin, and the documents of Sun President Li Vice President to the three eastern provinces were issued. They showed the comrades: This is a meeting for a great man to make contributions. Everyone was enthusiastic. They discussed with each other: The three eastern provinces are densely populated with mountains, and bandits come and go. Military and police are densely distributed. Today's affairs, the military and police without the encouragement of bandits, there is no chance to launch. Bandits without the surveillance of military and police, there is no way to control. We should use bandits to contain the military and police, and use military and police to control bandits. Everyone said it was good. So Tao Yuchun, Wang Wenfeng, etc. joined the police. Zhuang Yushu, Yao Xiuyun, etc. joined the army. Wang Zechen, Li Fanwu, etc. combined local groups. Gu Xiuzhai and others recruited bandits. So Tian Bianyang and others, a large number of Liu Han's people, sincerely accepted the agreement to wait. Li Jiaao, the chief of Binjiang Dao, and Yao Peizhen, the commander, all communicated with the funds. Tingyue then served as the foreign affairs official and obtained the recognition of neutrality from various consuls. They then pulled down the dragon flag and changed it to the five-color flag to celebrate the restoration. The Self-Government Office was established to convene officials, gentry, military police, merchants, scholars, and the common people to discuss government affairs, eliminate harsh taxes, release prisoners, and protect the people and merchants. The order was orderly. Qichang was not surprised. Everyone called long live. Zhao Erxun and others heard of it and hurriedly changed the flag to protect themselves. Later, they heard that the Qing court abdicated and the north and south ceased fighting. The Governor of Jilin, Chen Zhaochang, hoped to be the governor and was jealous of the partisans. He used the surrendered general Yao Peizhen as his old department. He instigated an unexpected attack on the people's army. The battle lasted all day. Ammunition was exhausted and reinforcements were cut off. Tingdong and Tingyue died in the end. Those who died together were Tao Yuchun, Wang Zechen, Li Fanwu, and more than ten others. The people's army in various places lost their leaders and mostly dispersed automatically. However, they still kept their promises not to disturb the people. And they agreed to change their behavior, saying: I can't bear to be the legacy of the Liang brothers. Binjiang has always been a place where bandits gather. Residents must be prepared when they go out. Only during the revolution did the bandits keep their promises and restrain themselves. The people of Binjiang still think about it today. Tingdong has a son, named Dazong. Tingyue has a son named Daxin. Both can inherit the legacy of their ancestors. And Tinghuai ran for the country and engaged in revolution. For thirty years, he has never slackened. But his family has declined because of this, to the point where he cannot afford food and clothing. Tinghuai did not care about it at all. He often said: Forgetting the family for the country, shouldn't a person of ambition be like this? His breadth of mind is like this. I am sad about the encounters of the two martyrs. I am even more impressed by Tinghuai's ambition. Therefore, I specifically present it to the world so that future generations can learn from it.

Remembering Yang Guifei's Lychee 209

— Chan Tui

Although I don't boast about my travels overseas, saying that my footprints have traveled all over China's famous mountains, and that my appetite has tasted the famous products of various places, but as far as the places I have been to, the word "half" in "footprints halfway around the world" still has room for maneuvering. Not to mention food. Just take lychee for example. I am from Sichuan, born in Beiping, grew up in Zhejiang, and have traveled north, south, east, and west. As long as I have free time, I say that two secretaries write manuscripts. This travelogue may be comparable to a famous mountain record.

I entered Sichuan with the army in the fifth year of the Republic of China and was stationed in Jialing in the sixth year of the Republic of China. The mountains and rivers of Jialing are the best in the world. Therefore, there is a conch-like couplet on the city gate. "Three hundred miles of Jialing, twelve buildings in the garden." Emperor Xuanzong of Tang entered Sichuan. He loved the mountains and rivers of Jialing. He once ordered Wu Daozi to draw three hundred miles of Jialing on a screen. The mountains and rivers of Jialing cannot be moved to Shanghai. When I say that the mountains and rivers of Jialing are dark green, it is just a sentence and cannot be confirmed. Even if there are photographic equipment, it can only obtain its appearance and cannot obtain its spirit. But because of Emperor Xuanzong of Tang's love for Wu Daozi's paintings, those who see it will surely believe it without words.

Let's talk about these twelve buildings. The first is the Phoenix Tower. It is the birthplace of the Golden Wheel Emperor of the Great Zhou Dynasty. This tower was specially built as a memorial. The tower is three feet high. There is a jade bell hanging on it. The jade bell is a rare treasure in the world. The words cast on the bell were all made by Empress Wu. It can be used for textual research.

The second is Yang Guifei Tower. Yang Guifei's father, Yang Yuanzhen, was the household secretary of Lizhou in Shu. Lizhou is now Zhongxian. The tower is behind the prefectural office. According to legend, it is the residence of the household secretary. Yang Guifei once planted hundreds of lychee trees herself. Now it is still a garden. The lychee has a red line in the middle of the waist, so it is also called "One Pinch of Red." Yang Guifei entered the palace and was made a noble concubine. Emperor Xuanzong specially ordered the governor of Lizhou to set up post relays. Therefore, there is a poem by the Tang people: "A rider of red dust smiles for the concubine. No one knows that lychee is coming." That is, Hong Fangsi's Palace of Eternal Life has a long tune singing about Yang Guifei's lychee. It can be seen that Yang Guifei's lychee is a famous product of Sichuan.

In May of the seventh year of the Republic of China, I once served as the acting governor of Zhongxian. I was in office for forty-seven days. What political achievements can be said? But for Yang Guifei's lychee, the garden is behind the tree, and it is produced every other year. The days I was in office were just when the lychee was first ripe. If it were in the former Qing Dynasty, it would have been a tribute. The county official would have been exhausted. How dare he eat one? Now it is the Republic of China. The county official is bigger than an ox. The agricultural products of the four villages can still be forcibly owned by the officials. Not to mention the lychee of this office. Every time I had free time, I invited three or five colleagues to cook wine in the garden and pick fresh lychee from the trees. The beauty of the color and taste, and the freshness of the water, truly deserve the name of Yang Guifei. Every time I eat it, I can get hundreds of them. Comparing it with the lychee sold in Shanghai, the difference is no less than that between heaven and earth. That's why I bought a basket of lychee today when I entered the market. Although it is said to be fresh fruit that has just arrived in Shanghai, it is not as delicious as the fresh lychee picked from the trees.

Storytelling Rotary Club

Three Eras (5) 210

— Zhang Henshui

Zhang Xiao San'er said. "Okay, the police look down on me. Even my own wife looks down on me. I rented the house. I paid the rent. Why do you dare to lock the door and not let me in?" Speaking, he kicked the door with one foot. With a thud, it kicked open. He jumped in. He stared at her and said. "You eat my food. You drink my drink. You dare to quarrel with me. I'm going to beat you. Anyway, rickshaw pullers can't beat the police. At worst, we'll go to the police station together." He scolded all the way. He walked in all the way. He saw the white stove against the wall. The fire was burning brightly. The small iron pot on top had a layer of steamer. There was a rattling sound in the pot. A burst of white steam rushed out. From this white steam, there was a smell of corn bread. Seeing this, the corn bread was steaming in the pot. It was about to be cooked. Zhang Xiao San's stomach was starving. When he smelled this smell, he couldn't help but drool. So he walked forward. He lifted the steamer lid. He saw the heat filled the air. More than a dozen fist-sized corn breads were steaming in the steamer. They were golden yellow. He brushed a layer of soda on it. It showed that it was steamed through. He pulled a pair of chopsticks from the chopstick holder on the wall. Just as he was about to insert it into the steamer. Zhang Er Sao grabbed it. She covered the steamer and pressed it with her hand. Don't be busy. I ask you. Did you throw down the money to buy corn flour yesterday? (Note: Corn flour is the powder ground from corn. It is used to make corn bread.) Zhang Xiao San said. "What if I didn't?" Zhang Er Sao said. "That's it. You said I eat your food. I wear your clothes. This shows that I didn't eat your food. This is the money I made from sewing work in the tailor shop. (Note: All work is generally called work in plain language, such as a barber going out to shave heads is called external work.) You are eating my food. What should I do?" Zhang Xiao San said. "You eat my food every day. It's nothing for me to eat one meal from you." Zhang Er Sao said. "Eat one meal. You calculate. How many meals have you eaten from me in the past ten days? You have money to go to the teahouse. Listen to the storytellers' nonsense. When you get home, Xue Rengui's expedition to the east. Huang Tianba's marriage proposal. You still have to learn it for three days and three nights. You are in your twenties and thirties. You still need your wife to support you." She rambled on and on. She said this long paragraph. Her hand was still pressing the steamer lid. She didn't let Zhang Xiao San lift it. Zhang Xiao San took a short stool. He stuffed it under his butt. He squatted down. He sat down. He saw Zhang Er Sao standing there. She raised her hands. She reached out to touch the messy hair on her head. She raised her two big sleeves. It revealed her two big white breasts. They hung down in a daze. He couldn't help but laugh. Zhang Er Sao saw him smile. She had more confidence. She held a broken rattan chair. She sat diagonally to him. She held the hem of her clothes with both hands. She turned it upwards. She fanned it like a fan. The higher she fanned it. The hem of her clothes turned up. It revealed her navel.

A Comparative Study of "The Liar" 211

— Yun Xian

The famous play by the Fudan Drama Society in its 11th public performance.

In the plot of Jones's "The Liar," the author's soul is hidden. And this magical soul plays a smiling character. He proclaims to the masses all over the world. Divorce is unfortunate. Lying is impossible. Lin Wangxian, who has experienced the world and tasted all kinds of hardships and advises his infatuated friend Zhang Jingkai to turn back, is clearly the author himself who has seen through the hearts of the world. Lin Wangxian here believes that seducing a married woman, although it is out of a sacred spiritual love, is also inappropriate. It seems that Jones, who is Zhang Jingkai, is a moralist who wears the mask of etiquette and teaches. Free love, in the present era, is a sacred event recognized by everyone. It should not be subject to any oppression. Whether she or he is a married woman or a married man. If there is no love between husband and wife, then this marriage built on dead love does not need to be maintained. If all the clear-headed people think this way. Then, in this way, Jones is a member of the old era with a corrupt mind. There is no need to perform his works again today.

But it is not so.

What kind of person is Jones? Is he a maintainer of old etiquette? Slowly. Please turn over and read "Magal and His Lost Angel," which was created two years earlier than "The Liar." This script directly attacks the old etiquette. It attacks the church with blood. The attack on the old etiquette and old morality in "Magal and His Lost Angel" is ten times more intense than the criticism of the impropriety of divorce in "The Liar."

The author in "The Liar" has no sympathy for Zhang Jingkai, who is wholeheartedly and sincerely in love, and drives others into the sea of ​​bitter love and cannot be saved. At the end of the fourth act, the audience fully sympathizes with and is moved by Zhang Jingkai's distress at this time, when his lover suddenly leaves without saying goodbye. They even feel sorry for him. But the author finally sends him to Nanyang, where there is only bitter heat and hard work. In such a place, the author fully shows that he is a cold and unfeeling person. But please also read "Magal and His Lost Angel," gentlemen who think so. The author in this book, from the same pen, is full of enthusiasm for life.

Now. Comparing the two immortal masterpieces that Jones contributed to the world of drama at the same time. We only understand that he is not a maintainer of old morality. He is not an unfeeling and indifferent person. Then we have to ask. Why in "The Liar." The author showed the opposite tendency to that in "Magal and His Lost Angel." If I am allowed to make a judgment in the following sentence. This is the opposite writing method of the great writer Jones. It is the place where his skills change. It is also his perverted means.

In any case. The author said the following through Lin Wangxian's mouth. It is the only loud warning to the men and women in China who are currently in the divorce craze.

"Don't think that once you get married. You can leave your wife alone and not care about her. You can't. You have now married the most beautiful woman in Shanghai. But if you don't continue to love her. Someone else will love her. There is nothing to say. This is the tragedy of life." (Min Shi's note: The play has been translated and directed by Mr. Zhu Duanjun of the Fudan Drama Society. It will be performed at the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Association on the thirteenth and fourteenth of this month. The Fudan Drama Society is well-known. This performance is its eleventh.)

US Cotton Weekend Statistics 219

A New York dispatch from the 12th reported on the cotton market during the week. At the beginning of the week, the cotton market reached new lows due to the weakness of the securities market and favorable reports on the southern climate. Those who had bought futures sold them again during the recent rebound, but the decline in value did indeed increase the demand from domestic and foreign traders, and short covering also caused prices to rise. The current market is certainly below cost, so price declines are sufficient to attract purchases by long positions, but buyers rarely indicate that they will follow the upward trend when prices rise. The climate in the cotton region is generally favorable, and cotton production is progressing well. However, there are many reports of bollworms in Garu Lana and southern Texas, which are said to be a major threat to the new cotton crop, and this is causing great concern. The closing of long positions for July futures was absorbed by spot traders to cover their short positions in far-month contracts.

Yesterday's market at Xinzha remained stagnant. Few stores opened in the morning, and appetite was even weaker. The opening price gradually declined, with weak buying leading to lower prices, indirectly affecting cargo by boat. Continuous arrivals from the west increased supply, but with the Dragon Boat Festival approaching, firms were settling accounts and the river storage was full. The hot weather made it difficult to store cargo for long, and rice was prone to heating, so the market lacked vitality. Medium and lower grades of Northern Japonica rice saw the least trading, with prices dropping by 0.2-0.3 yuan. Early and late rice, as well as foreign rice, were neglected, and prices fell by 0.1-0.2 yuan. Sales of white yuan rice were slow, and the trend continued downward.

Yesterday in South Shanghai, 16th and 17th grade rice arrived from the lower river region, but sales were sluggish. Changshu and Xixi premium japonica rice and Suzhou white japonica rice continued to decline, with premium rice down 0.2 yuan and lower grades down 0.4 yuan. The decline in early and late rice slowed, with opening prices down around 0.3 yuan. Foreign dujian rice was not in short supply, and medium and lower grades saw the most improvement in trading. White yuan rice sold well, and the trend was unlikely to loosen. Buying was weak and sales were flat. Arrivals from Anhui and Jiangxi were dwindling, and inventory was limited. Sporadic trading was minimal, and prices were uniquely stable.

Improved Outlook for Flour Futures 222

Yesterday in the flour market, after the opening in the morning, the market for each month was good due to favorable weather and a shift in sentiment among inland traders. Although foreign wheat prices had rebounded by around 0.2-0.4 yuan, most traders did not change their minds. After the opening, selling pressure increased, and market prices gradually declined, falling by 0.1-0.2 yuan compared to the previous day's closing price. However, at the opening in the afternoon, the market initially fluctuated, but due to the hot and muggy weather, people again speculated that heavy rain was coming, and suddenly short covering occurred, so the market strengthened again. However, the actual sales for this month were stagnant, so the outcome remained the same, as the reported price for Tianjin current flour by naval vessel was still 3.07 yuan. As a result, this month was down a small 0.25 li, July was up 0.25 li, August was unchanged, September was up 0.25 li, October was down a small 0.25 li, and November was down a small 0.25 li.

Wheat Futures in Flux 223

Yesterday in the wheat futures market, after the opening in the morning and afternoon, the market for each month generally tended to fluctuate. Although foreign wheat prices had improved in the morning, prices for both near and far contracts fell by around 0.1-0.2 fen due to weak sentiment. In the afternoon, the market naturally followed the large decline and small rebound in the flour market, and stabilized slightly. However, the new wheat situation this year showed that about 90% had already been harvested in the Jiangnan region, and although there was still 20-30% remaining in Jiangbei, it would not hinder the future. Furthermore, the quality of the wheat was better than in previous years, so if the standard was raised too much, it would inevitably lead to an influx of current goods in the future. As a result, this month was unchanged, July was up by 0.1, August, September, and October were unchanged, and November was down by a small 0.1. The current wheat market was characterized by initial attempts at packaging, which were not yet smooth. Yesterday, 4 liang of Chuzhou wheat was opened, totaling over 200 bags.

Foreign Long-Grain Rice Sales Sluggish and Expected to Soften 224

Yesterday, the foreign long-grain rice market was unusually quiet. No one inquired about foreign rice, and there were no sellers. There were no transactions in either futures or spot markets. Although foreign long-grain rice holders were willing to sell, buyers had absolutely no interest. The only transaction was by this street for 170 bags of late Jiangxi machine rice at 11.1 yuan. There were no other transactions, and the market remained sluggish.

Silk and Tea: Foreign Firms Still Find Silk Sales Difficult 225

Yesterday, foreign firms in the local silk market continued to struggle. Overseas Japanese silk prices remained lower than Chinese silk prices. Telegram inquiries to Shanghai were few. Chinese merchants were passive, and transactions were difficult. Only Jardine Matheson and other firms brought in 30 bales of Shanghai white filature silk, and Taisoo and other firms brought in 25 bales of white dried filature silk. Prices remained firm.

Flow of New Dried Cocoons from Jiangsu to Shanghai Continues Smoothly 226

The spring cocoon production in Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, and Zhenjiang was unusually poor, with less than 30% of the usual volume. Only about 30% of the cocoon shops opened compared to previous years, and the amount collected was generally not smooth. Currently, they are gradually closing down and processing the collected fresh cocoons for drying, and shipping them to Shanghai in batches by train. Temporary inspections and weighings are being conducted at the Maigen Road station of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway. Due to the poor harvest and small quantities of goods, only 500-600 bags are being transported to Shanghai each day, which is less than one-tenth of the previous year.

Transport of Wuyuan Crated Tea on the Gan River Still Obstructed 227

Wuyuan crated tea is usually exported via the waterway through Poyang and Jiujiang to Shanghai. Last year, due to banditry on the Yue-De line, the route was changed to land transport via Tunxi. Currently, the First Grade Precious Eyebrow teas from various firms are being crated and shipped in large quantities. However, due to concerns about unresolved banditry on the Gan River, which could lead to further losses, firms are cautiously deciding to continue using the old route via Tunxi. Although land transport increases costs, they are not concerned about this in order to ensure speed and avoid risks.

Bud Tea from Anhui is Emerging 228

This year's spring tea harvest in the counties of Wuyuan, Xiuning, and She in Anhui Province was poor, with production only about half of last year. As a result, the amount of tea purchased by the tea firms in Tunxi, Wuyuan, and She was mostly less than expected. The bud tea harvest is now expected to make up for the shortfall. In various regions, the buds are now emerging, with a slightly purple color and a fragrant taste. If the weather is clear for ten days, with dew every morning, good development can be expected. Farmers are treating the bud tea as a rare commodity, preparing to harvest and process only a limited amount. The price when it is released is expected to be higher than regular tea.

Shot-Sized Pearl Tea Sells Best in Europe 229

Yesterday, in the local tea market for foreign firms, Jinlong, Tongfu, Xiehe, and Jardine Matheson were showing strong interest in shot-sized pearl tea from the Ping Shui Tu Zhuang area. The highest price for top-grade pearl tea reached 110 taels, and the market price was quite firm. For Zhenmei tea from the Lu Zhuang area, Chinese and foreign traders were still unable to reach an agreement due to the large difference in market prices. No special prices were offered throughout the city. However, Jardine Matheson and Xiehe made slight purchases of Needle Eyebrow tea, with high-grade tea selling for 73 taels and low-grade tea selling for 32-33 taels, with no increases or decreases from the previous day.

Piece Goods: White Fabrics and Woolens Sell Exceptionally Well 230

The woolen fabric market has been relatively calm recently, with no unusual price fluctuations. Only summer white drill and white straight-tribute fabrics saw slight changes yesterday. Demand was strong, and inventories were low, so selling prices gradually increased. Door-to-door shops and small traders were adding inventory daily, but full-box transactions were rare. Mitsui goods were very popular, and other Western goods from Levy, Hoste, and Italian firms were also running out of stock. Yesterday, Mitsui white straight-tribute fabric sold for 4 taels, 6 qian, 5 fen, and white drill sold for a net price of 4 taels.

Fine Cloth Jumps by 1 Qian 231

The local cotton cloth market showed improvement again yesterday, with fine cloth making a leap forward. This was due to renewed activity from Tianjin traders and large-scale purchases from Sichuan traders, which caused a sudden surge in sentiment. Current goods were in short supply, and prices of all brands rose by around 1 qian. Blue Chicken reached 7 taels, 5 qian, 2 fen, 5 li in the afternoon. Blue Flying Fish was very scarce, selling for 7 taels, 9 qian, 7 fen, 5 li. Blue Double Fish sold for 7 taels, 7 qian, Yang Crane sold for 7 taels, 6 qian, 5 fen, and Hunter sold for 7 taels, 5 qian, 7 fen, 5 li. Blue Chicken was the most popular among all brands, with over 300 pieces purchased by Sichuan traders. Nine-pound cloth was the firmest among coarse cloths, reaching over 5 taels, 1 qian. Fine twill rose by 5 fen, and both Yih-Ho bleached cloth and plain cloth were firm.

In the Eastern piece goods market, Eastern goods were more active, and the demand from traders was unprecedented. In particular, Sichuan traders showed a sudden surge in demand, with over 50 pieces of hunting goose straight-tribute woolen fabric traded at 3 qian, 7 fen, 7 li, 5 hao. Purchases of fine drill were also significant, with Lake Pavilion at 3 qian, 4 fen, 5 li, and Jin Wengong at 3 qian, 3 fen, 5 li. Tianjin traders bought more Three Friends brand cloth, which sold for 3 qian, 3 fen, 5 li. Bleached cloth was added by many on this street, with Fu Hui at 12 taels, 4 qian, 5 fen, Ding Fu Jun San Shi at 11 taels, 9 qian, and Fu Shou San Xing at 11 taels, 1 qian. Striped Fu Silk and Striped Satin were consistently firm due to the gradual reduction in current goods. Western goods were extremely scarce, and lower grades of Yuanfang's Yuan Yu Silk were almost non-existent.

Sugar Market: Coarse Granulated White Sugar Dips Slightly Before Rising 232

According to dispatches from sugar-producing regions yesterday, the current price of Cuban sugar remained at 1.3125, the price of New York sugar futures for September was 1.29, up one cent from the previous day, the price for December was 1.37, unchanged, and the prices for March and May of next year were 1.45 and 1.51, respectively, each up one cent. The current price of Javanese sugar was 8 guilders, and the price of sugar futures for July and August was 8.125, unchanged from the previous day. Trading at the public association market remained quiet. Trading in Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar was slightly more active, opening at 11 taels, 4 qian, 7 fen, 5 li. Due to the lack of suppliers, it then rose to 11 taels, 5 qian. The market situation was particularly flat. No. 20 medium granulated white sugar was 10 taels, 08 qian, 5 fen, with very few buyers. Trading in Japanese sugar was also sporadic, with ER mark at 11 taels, 7 qian, YP mark at the same price, YT mark at 10 taels, 3 qian, and YRO mark at 10 taels, 09 qian, 5 fen. The market outlook was stable. Trading in brand-name sugar was even quieter, with only Zhenxiang selling 1,000 bags of current coarse granulated white sugar at 11 taels, 5 qian. The trend was unremarkable.

Dried Goods: Sichuan Pickled Mustard Greens Have Reached Bottom 233

Due to a bumper crop and abundant supply of Sichuan pickled mustard greens this year, supply exceeded demand, and market prices have gradually declined. Prices have now reached the bottom, with middle-grade mustard greens only selling for 21-22 yuan, a difference of more than ten yuan from the highest price. Therefore, some in the industry are planning to buy and stockpile them, which may cause the market to improve slightly.

Hardware: New Lead Wire Sales Active Among Yangtze Traders 234

New lead wire of sizes 8, 10, 12, 13, and 14 has recently seen a surge in trading. It is reported that the buyers are mostly from the Yangtze River region, with some scattered demand from Tianjin traders. Due to supply falling short of demand, prices have risen sharply, estimated at 10-12 taels. However, as remaining inventory dries up, prices are expected to gradually increase further.
